The 98th Meeting of the Legislative Yuan 2

The Legislative Yuan held its 98th meeting at 8:00 AM today (the 28th). The attending members were Lü Zhiyi, Jiao Yitang, Shi Shangkuan, Chen Zhaoying, Lin Bin, Ma Yinchu, Dai Xiujun, Tao Xuan, Shao Yuanchong, Sun Jingya, Lou Tongsun, Wu Shangying, Zhang Zhihan, Wang Yongbin, Cai Xuan, Liu Guanxun, Lu Zhonglin, Liu Jixue, Luo Ding, Zeng Jie, Wei Tingsheng, Zhang Fengjiu, Chuan Bingchang, Chen Changheng, Zhu Hezhong, Liu Jingxin, Lu Yinong, Zheng Kaichen, and Wei Huai, totaling 29 people. The chair was Hu Hanmin. The matters for discussion were as follows: (1) Deliberation on whether the oath of office for the Secretary and other positions of the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs should use the civil official oath or the military officer oath. It was resolved to use the military officer oath. (2) The Labor Law Drafting Committee of the Yuan reported on the examination of the National Government's response to the Executive Yuan's submission regarding the Shanghai Special Municipality's request for interim measures to be stipulated before the differences in the new and old Labor-Management Dispute Resolution Law are resolved, and the draft implementation rules were reviewed by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. The Yuan decided to adopt the examination report. (3) The Labor Law Drafting Committee of the Yuan reported on the review of the various recommendations of the Third Plenary Session of the Third Central Executive Committee, including the Shanghai Special Municipality's request to the Central Government to issue various laws and regulations on labor savings and labor insurance to all regions. It was resolved to adopt the examination report. (4) The Legal System Committee of the Yuan reported on the amendment of Article 11, Paragraph 4 of the Legislative Yuan Organization Law. It was resolved to adopt the examination report.

Shandong Provincial Government Moves Office to Qingdao 3

Qingdao Correspondence: Due to changes in military strategy and in deference to the requests of consuls from various countries stationed in Jinan, the Shandong military and central army will no longer engage in combat near Jinan. From the night of the 24th, Han Fuqu ordered his troops to be transferred to the Jiaoji Railway line. The acting Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, Zhu Xi, and committee members Yuan Jiapu, He Siyuan, Yu Enbo, Cui Shijie, Chen Luanshu, Chen Mingyu, as well as important officials of the provincial government, also arrived in Qingdao at 6:00 AM on the 25th on a special train. Those who came together included the Mayor of Jinan, Zhao Jingshi, and the Chief of Staff of the Headquarters, Li Erkang. After arriving in Qingdao, the committee members temporarily borrowed a portion of Qingdao University's buildings to establish a temporary office and continue to perform the functions of the provincial government. They telegraphed the county magistrates, instructing them to continue to be responsible for all duties and report at any time. They also telegraphed the Central Government for instructions. The two telegrams are recorded below:

Telegram to the Central Government: The province of Shandong has declared that Chairman Chen has been ordered to go to the front lines to supervise the troops, and the military affairs of the entire province are entirely the responsibility of Commander-in-Chief Han. Han's troops have fought hard for over a month, repeatedly thwarting the enemy's advance. Recently, the enemy has launched a full-scale offensive, and the situation has changed abruptly. Han's troops began to retreat on the Yangri River. The official residence has a duty to defend, but there is no way to defend itself. After repeated deliberation, the Jinan Municipal Public Security Bureau Chief Gong Weijiang was instructed to be responsible for protecting the security of Chinese and foreign people in the city. The provincial government and its affiliated offices were ordered to assign personnel to be responsible for the safekeeping of documents and affairs. On the day (the 25th), at Chou time, the troops moved out of Jinan. Due to an obstacle on the Pingpu Railway line, troops were prepared to be used between Qingwei, so the government moved to Qingdao and temporarily stayed in a part of Qingdao University. The officials are inept and have lost the county seat, feeling deeply guilty and awaiting punishment. We believe that although northern Shandong and Jinan have unfortunately fallen, the order in the east, west, and south sides is still safe, and the political power needs to be unified. Moreover, the enemy's hasty invasion has not solidified its foundations, and Han's troops still have strength. We urgently wish to counterattack. If the central army provides immediate reinforcements, the strong city can be restored. Before receiving clear orders, we will temporarily continue to perform the functions of the provincial government in Qingdao, maintaining the hearts of the people of the entire province who desire governance and supporting the Central Government's determination of the great cause. Should the Shandong Provincial Government Administrative Office be established in Qingdao, or should we take the sea route to Jinjing and transfer to Yanzhou and Jining to follow the troops and promote their effectiveness to redeem ourselves? We await your instructions and will obey. Telegram to the counties: The various committee members of this government are following the troops. The previous telegram should have arrived. We have now moved to Qingdao City and established a temporary office in Qingdao University. The magistrates of each city and county should be actively responsible for all duties. If there are reports, they should be sent directly to the temporary office as needed (June 25th).

The War in Fujian Province Is About to Erupt Again 4

The Navy and Army Are Preparing to Advance and Suppress Lu's Troops

Fuzhou Correspondence: Since Lu's troops were completely defeated by Liu's troops in the Fujian province war, Liu's troops have only guarded the important mountain tops on the northwest two roads and have not advanced. For a time, a stalemate was formed. Everyday, naval seaplanes are sent to the enemy's position to drop bombs and warn them. Lu's troops are disturbed by this, and their morale is shaken. The troops stationed along the Minjiang River in the Ganzhe, Zhuqi, and Baisha areas have mostly retreated into the mountainous forests of the inland Yuangou, Dahu, and Xiaoluo villages for concealment. (Lu Xingrong's command post has also been moved from Baisha to Xiaoluo.) There is also no preparation for a counterattack. Therefore, it is widely rumored in society that the National Government has sent a telegram to Fujian ordering both sides to cease fighting first and wait for someone to be sent to investigate and then resolve the matter politically. Therefore, the general public is hopeful for peace, especially the merchants, who are the most eager. However, in the past three days, the situation has suddenly changed again. The National Government has clearly ordered the deprivation of Lu Xingbang's official position and ordered the navy and army to jointly suppress him. On the one hand, Chairman Jiang telegraphed Liu Heding to commend the officers and soldiers of his troops for repelling the rebellious masses and to encourage them to continue their efforts to eliminate the rebellious atmosphere. Various guns, ammunition, and special military equipment for mountain warfare requested by Liu's troops have been successively transported. A group of Northwest Army prisoners of war has been specially sent to Fujian to be incorporated into Liu's troops to supplement their strength. The division plans to reorganize these prisoners of war into a supplementary brigade, with Jiang Yan, the regimental commander who has been the most effective in supervising the battle on the northern road, promoted to brigade commander. Together with the original three brigades of Gui Zhenyuan, Liu Shangzhi, and Chen Wantai, there will be a total of four brigades, plus an artillery regiment, an engineering regiment, a machine gun battalion, and a special service battalion, with a total strength of over 22,000 men. At the same time, the ordnance of each battalion will be completely replenished. The machine guns and mortars have been the most effective in this operation. Each battalion is specially equipped with three machine guns and two mortars, and the wartime configuration has now been completed. As for the navy, the Central Government has clearly ordered the suppression of Lu, and it has joined forces with Liu's troops to advance in three routes: left, middle, and right. The left route will advance from Nangang to Yongtai, led by the navy. The middle route will advance from Beiling to Gutian, and the right route will advance from Xixiang to Minqing, both led by Liu's troops. Since the 22nd, Liu's troops have been successively moving the majority of the troops stationed in the city out of the northwest city to Beiling and Baisha. The navy also believes that the two existing seaplanes are insufficient and has specially transferred Chen Wenlin, the director of the Xiamen Naval Aircraft Office, to lead two fighter planes to the province to assist in the battle. They will arrive within three days, and the Donghu barracks has been designated as a temporary airport. Lu's troops have learned that the provincial authorities are about to launch a major offensive, so they have intercepted all the ships and sailboats traveling to and from the upper reaches of the provincial capital, prohibiting them from sailing downstream to cut off transportation, and have concentrated their forces below Shuikou to block the advance of the provincial troops. According to investigations, Lu's troops have now concentrated all their forces in the front to participate in the battle, including the five brigades of Lu Xinglao, Lu Xinming, Chen Rongbiao, Zhou Zhiqun, and Chen Guocai (the one who rebelled in Wuhu earlier). Only one brigade of Lu Xingming is defending the rear, which is not enough. However, the people in the northwest countryside of the province had successively moved back after the ceasefire on the 13th. Now that they see the tense situation, they have moved into the city again since the 22nd, carrying boxes and burdens, supporting the old and carrying the young, one after another (24th).

The War in Fujian Affects Upstream Freight 5

Upstream Business Circles Write to the General Chamber of Commerce to Appeal

Fuzhou Correspondence: Liu Heding's troops are now very active in their combat plans due to the central government's order to suppress Lu. Yesterday, an order was issued to all units to replenish any deficiencies in addition to the original military supplies, and high terrain was acquired in the Dabeiling area to set up fortifications. However, the various upstream river transport merchant guilds have written to the General Chamber of Commerce and the Commercial Research Institute to forward to the authorities, requesting that they find a way to restore traffic, as the military has affected freight transport and commerce is in crisis. In general, those who specialize in the upstream business are the first to bear the brunt of the river blockage and suffer the greatest losses, but the losses suffered by the upstream business are no less than the losses suffered by the provincial business, because the upstream business and the provincial business are related to each other. The upstream merchants' business, in addition to their own capital, is generally borrowed from provincial merchants for lending, advance payment, exchange, etc. The various goods are sold in the province to offset the debt to return the provincial merchants. Otherwise, the upstream business will be hurt, affecting the whole system, such as banks, money merchants, north-south shipping, tea, wood, paper, bamboo shoots, new goods, salt, rice, passenger transport, and river transport merchants, which are the limbs of the upstream business. The river transport is the most prosperous in the fourth, fifth, and sixth months. The blockage of the river during this peak season is a dangerous situation. I hope that the giants of the city's business community will quickly find a way to provide relief. Fortunately, the upstream and downstream transport ships have been opened, and those that are blocked along the way, such as rice, tea, wood, salt, paper, bamboo shoots, dried fruits, fish, cloth, flour, oil, grain, foreign goods, and other bulk goods, as well as postal drafts that are blocked along the way, amount to no less than hundreds of thousands of yuan. After the exact figures have been investigated, they will be reported.

The Case of Japanese Soldiers Crushing Yang Ruiwen Is Resolved 6

Hankou Correspondence: The case of Japanese soldiers stationed in Hankou driving an unlicensed car at 2:00 PM on the 10th of this month and crushing Yang Ruiwen, a sergeant squad leader of the General Headquarters Hankou Camp, in the French Concession has been resolved after repeated negotiations by the municipal government. The Japanese side has acknowledged the three items of apology, compensation, and punishment of the murderer. Today (the 27th), it was officially resolved. The details of the negotiations in this case are recorded below. After the incident occurred, the camp immediately sent a letter to the municipal government requesting serious negotiations with the Japanese consulate. The original letter stated: "Our camp soldier Zhao Ruiwen was killed instantly at 2:00 PM on June 10th while on official duty in the French Concession by a reckless Japanese military vehicle. Cases involving Chinese and foreign nationals in Hankou are now handled by your government. The body of the soldier has been examined by the court and is still at the scene of the incident. The offending vehicle has been released by the French police. However, after serious negotiations by Secretary Wang of our camp, the Japanese consul personally signed his name to be responsible and agreed to be summoned at any time. The French police agreed to return the vehicle to the Japanese consul. Because this involves international negotiations, we are sending this letter to request that you promptly send personnel to conduct serious negotiations on compensation for the family and burial of the deceased, and must be generous to appease the wronged soul." After receiving the letter, the municipal government immediately checked and rescinded the post-disaster arrangements of the Negotiation Office, and in order to avoid all formalities, it appointed Wu Guozhen, the director of the Finance Bureau, as its representative to negotiate with the Japanese consulate. The Japanese Consul Tanaka received Representative Wu, who presented three demands to the Japanese Consul: (1) The Japanese military attaché should formally apologize to our authorities; (2) The deceased should be compensated generously; (3) The culprit should be severely punished. The Japanese Consul expressed acceptance and sent the naval attaché and army attaché to the camp to apologize to Director He. The amount of compensation was discussed several times without reaching an agreement. Later, Mayor Liu sent Li Boren, the director of the Health Bureau, to contact the Japanese Consul again. It was decided that the Japanese side would compensate 500 yuan and punish the culprit to close the case. Mayor Liu immediately reported the solution to Director He of the camp and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting instructions. Director He immediately expressed his agreement, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent two replies, one stating: "Now that your office has negotiated this case, the Japanese naval attaché has apologized to me and admitted to compensation. Please continue to negotiate on the spot to resolve it." The second stated: "The death of Yang Ruiwen in this car accident was indeed caused by the driver's negligence, but if Director He considers the various terms agreed to by the Japanese side to be feasible, please settle it accordingly." After receiving the replies from the camp and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the municipal government sent a letter to the Japanese Consul stating: "Regarding the case of the vehicle of your country's navy crushing Yang Ruiwen on June 10th in the local French Concession, the consul has agreed to provide a compensation fee of 500 silver dollars in addition to the clothing and coffin expenses, which shows great consideration for diplomatic relations and compassion for the deceased. Director Li Boren has been sent to your office to represent everything, and we hope you will accept and handle it." The Japanese side also replied in writing, and Japanese Consul Tanaka escorted Representative Li back to the municipal government with 500 yuan in cash and clothing and coffin expenses. The letter stated: "Regarding the case of the vehicle used by the local Japanese naval soldiers colliding with the bicycle ridden by Yang Ruiwen, a soldier of the camp, on June 10th, in the local French Concession, causing Yang Ruiwen's death, we offer our condolences to the deceased and the naval side will provide the bereaved family with a compensation fee of 500 yuan to resolve this case. This consul-general has previously discussed this matter with your mayor's representative, Director Li, and we have reached an agreement. We have received your government's letter No. 1657 dated the 24th of this month stating that your mayor has also agreed, etc. We are now sending 500 silver dollars and hope that you will check and forward them. Now that this case has been resolved, neither party will raise any demands on this matter in the future, whether public or private." After receiving the letter, the municipal government deposited the compensation with the camp for verification and transfer, and reported it to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for record (June 27).

The Hankou Municipal Government Will Be Reorganized on a Fixed Date 7

The Municipal Council Passes Organizational Regulations

After receiving the order to reorganize according to the new organization law, the Hankou Special Municipal Government immediately began planning and drafting organizational regulations, which were passed by the municipal council on the 26th and decided to implement on July 1st. The organizational regulations are recorded below: (Article 1) These regulations are formulated in accordance with the provisions of the Municipal Organization Law. (Article 2) This municipal government is named the Hankou Municipal Government and is directly under the National Government Executive Yuan in accordance with the provisions of Article 1 of the Municipal Organization Law. (Article 3) The area of this city is the area of the former Hankou Special Municipality. (Article 4) This municipal government shall manage the administrative affairs of the entire city and supervise its subordinate organs and autonomous bodies in accordance with the provisions of Article 11 of the Municipal Organization Law. (Article 5) This municipal government shall have one mayor to direct and supervise its subordinate officials. (Article 6) This municipal government shall have two councilors, appointed or recommended, to manage the drafting and review of municipal regulations or orders. (Article 7) This municipal government may employ specialized technical personnel as needed. (Article 8) This municipal government shall temporarily establish the following bureaus and offices: (1) Secretariat; (2) Social Affairs Bureau; (3) Public Safety Bureau; (4) Finance Bureau; (5) Public Works Bureau; (6) Education Bureau; (7) Health Bureau. Detailed rules for the operation of each bureau and office shall be determined separately. (Article 9) The Secretariat shall have one secretary-general, appointed or recommended, one to three secretaries, thirty to forty section chiefs and clerks, with section chiefs recommended or appointed and clerks appointed. (Article 10) The Secretariat shall manage documents, general affairs, and other matters not entrusted to the management of the various bureaus. (Article 11) The Social Affairs Bureau shall have one director, appointed or recommended, one secretary, five section chiefs recommended, two inspectors recommended or appointed, and fifty to fifty-five section chiefs and clerks, with section chiefs recommended or appointed and clerks appointed. (Article 12) The responsibilities of the Social Affairs Bureau are as follows: 1. Household registration and personnel registration matters; 2. Establishment of facilities for childcare, elderly care, poverty alleviation, and disaster relief; 3. Food reserves and regulation matters; 4. Improvement and protection of agriculture, industry, and commerce; 5. Labor administration matters; 6. Protection and prohibition of afforestation, land reclamation, fishing, and hunting; 7. Supervision of privately-operated public utilities; 8. Organization and guidance of cooperative societies and mutual aid undertakings; 9. Customs reform matters. (Article 13) The Public Safety Bureau shall have one director, appointed or recommended, one to three secretaries, one chief inspector recommended, ten to twelve inspectors recommended or appointed, and fifty to sixty section chiefs and clerks, with section chiefs recommended or appointed and inspectors and clerks appointed. (Article 14) The responsibilities of the Public Safety Bureau are as follows: 1. Public security matters; 2. Fire protection matters. (Article 15) The Finance Bureau shall have one director, appointed or recommended, one secretary, five section chiefs, one to two technicians-in-chief recommended, two to four inspectors recommended or appointed, section chiefs recommended or appointed, clerks appointed, six to eight technicians and twelve to fourteen technical assistants appointed. (Article 16) The responsibilities of the Finance Bureau are as follows: 1. Financial revenue and expenditure and budget and final account matters; 2. Management and disposal of public property; 3. Operation and management of public enterprises; 4. Land administration matters. (Article 17) The Public Works Bureau shall have one director, appointed or recommended, one secretary, four section chiefs, five to eight technicians-in-chief recommended, twenty-five to twenty-eight section chiefs and clerks, with section chiefs recommended or appointed and clerks appointed, and fourteen to sixteen technicians and technical assistants appointed. (Article 18) The responsibilities of the Public Works Bureau are as follows: 1. Construction and repair of public buildings, parks, public sports fields, public cemeteries, etc.; 2. Guidance and prohibition of citizens' construction; 3. Roads, bridges, canals, embankments, and other public civil engineering projects; 4. River channels, port affairs, and ship administration matters. (Article 19) The Education Bureau shall have one director, appointed or recommended, one secretary, three section chiefs recommended, two to four supervisors recommended or appointed, and thirty to forty section chiefs and clerks, with section chiefs recommended or appointed and clerks appointed. (Article 20) The responsibilities of the Education Bureau are as follows: 1. Education matters; 2. All cultural matters. (Article 21) The Health Bureau shall have one director, appointed or recommended, one secretary, three section chiefs, two technicians-in-chief recommended, two inspectors recommended or appointed, and twenty to thirty section chiefs and clerks, with section chiefs recommended or appointed and clerks appointed, and two to four technicians-in-chief appointed. (Article 22) The responsibilities of the Health Bureau are as follows: 1. Public health matters; 2. Establishment and prohibition of hospitals, vegetable markets, slaughterhouses, and public entertainment venues, etc. (Article 23) This municipal government and its subordinate bureaus and offices may employ employees as appropriate. (Article 24) This municipal government and its subordinate bureaus and offices may establish affiliated agencies as needed. (Article 25) This municipal government shall establish a municipal council in accordance with the provisions of Article 24 of the Municipal Organization Law, which shall be composed of the mayor, councilors, and bureau directors. After the establishment of the Municipal Assembly, three to five representatives may be mutually elected by the municipal councilors to attend the municipal council meetings. The secretary-general of this municipal government shall attend the municipal council meetings. (Article 26) All matters stipulated in Article 25 of the Municipal Organization Law shall be decided by the municipal council. (Article 27) The municipal council shall meet once a week, convened by the mayor, who shall serve as the chairman. (Article 28) Detailed rules for the municipal council shall be determined separately. (Article 29) If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, the mayor may submit them to the municipal council for discussion and submit them to the Executive Yuan for amendment. (Article 30) These regulations shall be implemented on the date of approval and promulgation by the Executive Yuan (June 27).

Important News 2

Guangdong Merchants Organize Fuguo Company 9

Mining Coal in Jiang District, Northeast

The Guangzhou General Chamber of Commerce, in conjunction with the Coal Industry and Silk Industry Research Society and overseas Chinese, has organized a coal mining company named Fuguo Company to mine the Jiang mining area in the Northeast. This is an innovative move in establishing industries, and it is very important for counteracting foreign coal, providing for daily use, and employing workers. According to responsible officials of the company, the mining areas in Qujiang County, including Xishui, Simaoping, Matiwo, Laohuchong, Dalingdongshui, and the mining areas in Lechang County, including Yangxi, Chulingjiao, Jigongshan, and Tuzhuling, have been repeatedly surveyed and tested by the famous coal mining engineer Rong Jintong. Hong Kong government chemist Du Wei analyzed the coal quality in March of this year and found it to be high-quality white coal. Furthermore, British mining engineer McJoe surveyed the area several years ago and stated that the area has abundant mineral resources. Based on the Xiangri Xiexing Coal Mine (located in front of the company's mining site in Matiwo), which produces 15,000 tons per month, the reserves are sufficient for more than fifty years of mining. The mining sites now developed by our company have ten times the output of that mine. Furthermore, in February of this year, the Construction Department sent personnel to conduct a joint survey with the county and approved the mining. It has been found that the above-mentioned coal mines mostly produce smokeless white coal, suitable for machinery factories and cooking fuel, similar to the mines in Hongji, French Indochina, and superior to the mixed coal from Tokyo and Haiphong. According to recent surveys, the annual consumption of this white coal is approximately 100,000 tons in Guangzhou, approximately 500,000 to 600,000 tons in Shanghai, approximately 100,000 tons in Shantou and Xiamen, approximately 200,000 tons in Hong Kong, and approximately 600,000 to 700,000 tons in Japan, totaling over 1.8 million tons. Although Henan Province's Fu'an Company produces white coal, it is far from the south and difficult to supply. It is regrettable that the huge demand is monopolized by French Indochina's Hongji white coal and Quji, Maoji, Jibu, Dongxiang, and other mixed coals. It is also regrettable that the same white coal is produced everywhere in the Beijiang area of Guangdong, but due to various difficulties, the goods are abandoned on the ground. The purpose of our company's initiation of mining is not only to meet the needs of industry and civilian use in the province but also to focus on developing foreign trade, transporting and selling to other provinces and foreign countries, so as to resist foreign goods and promote domestic products. It is estimated that the mining areas have been submitted for opening, and there is also oil coal sufficient for long-term use by ships, trains, electrical machinery plants, silk factories, etc. The function of white coal briquettes and oil coal is equivalent, and it can also be made into smokeless coal briquettes to replace firewood and solid carbon, which is truly beneficial to the national economy and the daily life of the people. The concern is that the history of mining in Guangdong has been repeated. If no measures are taken to remedy the causes of failure, then the act of benefiting the country and the people is simply empty talk. Beijiang and Guangzhou are neighboring lands, arriving in the evening after a morning departure, but the calculated cost of mining is not as good as the cheap price of foreign coal brought in by sea, with heavy taxes and odd transportation fees. Both are fatal injuries to the operation of domestic coal. With heavy costs, transportation is naturally slow. No one in this province pays attention to it, let alone shipping it overseas. As a result, they can only wait to die and let foreign coal be imported. Our company has requested the General Chamber of Commerce to list the minimum requirements, one of which falls within the scope of the Ministry of Finance: (A) In addition to paying land tax for the mining area and wellhead tax for mineral products, our company's coal will be exempt from all taxes and levies at checkpoints when transported for sale in the province, and all counties will be ordered to strictly prohibit additional levies under the guise of local public welfare and police expenses. (B) The Fushun Coal Mine only pays an export tax of one penny for transporting coal, and all other import taxes and levies are waived. Coal mines opened in Qingdao and other places pay only one penny for export tax and half tax of five cents at the port of entry, and no other taxes are levied. The purpose of our company's coal mining is to compete with foreign coal, not only to stop the leak but also to vigorously promote it abroad, and it is not enough to seriously reduce costs to compete with imported coal. It is proposed to give special preferential treatment and follow the example of the Fushun Coal Mine. In addition to paying the regular tax of one penny, all sales to other provinces will no longer be taxed. The second falls within the scope of the Ministry of Railways: The government has many precedents for reducing transportation costs to maintain domestic products. The Shandong Zhongxing Coal Mining Company's railway coal transportation is charged by the railway bureau with the highest rate of seven cents of ocean per ton per kilometer and the lowest rate of five cents and five mills of ocean per ton per kilometer. Within 240 kilometers, it is set at six cents and five mills per ton per kilometer. The length of the route is similar to that from Guangzhou to Shaoguan. Our company follows the precedent and proposes to stipulate that the freight rate be six cents and five mills of ocean per ton per kilometer, and the railway bureau will provide transportation vehicles. If our company provides vehicles, then the freight rate will be calculated at five cents and five mills per ton per kilometer, and the Yuehan Railway Administration will be ordered to handle it according to the proposed freight rate. The third falls within the scope of both the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining and the Ministry of Railways: Please exempt all domestic Taiping San Pass, Huangsha Li Factory, etc. from levying tariffs in addition to paying customs duties on our company's mining and transportation machinery, rails, carts, locomotives, and other mining and transportation equipment. As for railway freight, please also follow the precedent of the Zhongxing mining area and reduce it by half. The fourth falls within the scope of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining: Please follow the Shandong Zhongxing Coal Mine's articles of association, which stipulate that traditional methods of mining are not allowed within ten miles and that no company using the same machinery is allowed within one hundred miles, so as to avoid disputes between each other during mining. The above-mentioned items are purely for the purpose of resisting foreign coal invasion and encouraging the promotion of domestic coal at home and abroad, and for the sake of developing industry and maintaining civilian use, there is nothing more urgent than this.

New Survey of Tusi and Tuguan in Sichuan 10

The positions have historically been hereditary, only with the Ministry adding appointments to show restraint.

Internally, everything will be planned to be merged with the current system.

Sichuan Province has recently implemented the abolition of Daos and reorganized county governments. In addition to the original 146 counties, two new counties, Baoxing and Ningnan, have been added. The three Tuns of Chonghua, Fubian, and Suijing in western Sichuan are now directly under the jurisdiction of the provincial government and are still waiting for discussion on reorganization and merger. The titles of Tusi and Tuguan under the jurisdiction of the various border counties are numerous and will also be comprehensively planned and merged separately to conform to the current system. According to the survey by the provincial government, the names of the various Tusi, Tuguan, and Tuzu are very detailed and are disclosed as follows:

Pingwu County, Western Fan and Tuban, established one Tusi Tongpan, one Tusi Changguansi, and one Tusi Zhishi.

Mao County, Qiang ethnic group, established three Changguansi, two Xunjiansi, and one Anfusi.

Wenchuan, Tanggute ethnic group, established one Wasi Tusi and one Xuanweishi Si.

Songpan County, Man, Rong, Qiang, and Guo ethnic groups, established one Changguansi and one Minzhengsi, thirteen Tusi Shoubei, eight Tusi Qianzong, and each one Tusi Bazong Waiwei.

Lifan County, Tuban, established four Tusi, three Changguansi, and one Xuanweishi.

Maogong County, Yi ethnic group, established two Tusi, ten Datouren, and ten Xiaotouren.

Xichang County, Guo Luo, established five Changguansi, nine Qianhu, and twelve Baihu.

Mianning County, Western Fan and Guo Luo, established one Tusi and seven Baihu. Zhaojue County, Yi ethnic group, established one Xuanfusi and eleven Tusi Mu. Yuejun County, Guo Luo and Western Fan, established one Xuanfusi and one Tusi Dusi, and two Tusi Guan.

Yanbian County, Miao, Fan, and Guo Luo, established one Bingmasi and one Changguansi, two Tusi Qianhu, and twenty Datou.

Tianquan County, Tusi Fan, established one Xuanweishi Si.

Ebian County, Guo Luo and Yi ethnic groups, established five Tusi Qianhu and three Tusi Mu, and seventeen Tusi Baihu.

Yanyuan County, Western Fan and Zhou Yi, established two Anfusi and one Bingmasi, three Tusi Qianhu, twenty Tusi Ba Si, six Tusi Baihu, and nine Tusi Mu.

Mabian County, Black and White Guo Yi, established one Tusi Qianhu, one Tusi Mu, and one Qiuzhang each.

Leibo County, Black and White Yi, established one Changguansi, thirteen Tusi Qianhu, and forty-two Tusi Baihu.

Gulan County, Guo Luo and Miao Yi, established eight Tusi Mu.

Qijiang County, Luo Na and Qinghong Miao ethnic groups, established three Tusi Mu.

Nanchuan County, Miao ethnic group, established one Tusi Mu.

The above-mentioned positions of Tusi and Tuguan have historically been hereditary, with the Ministry adding appointment certificates to show restraint. Because they do not conform to the new system, the Ministry of Interior has requested the Sichuan Provincial Government to temporarily add appointments and separately formulate unified measures for submission to the Ministry for approval.

Hangzhou Quick News 11

This morning at four o'clock, a fire broke out at the Wang Rixing chopstick shop at the entrance of Dajing Lane, spreading to more than twenty houses, burning to death four men and women.

In order to unify the organization of all merchants in Zhejiang Province, the Provincial Training Department plans to send Xu Da and thirteen others to Hangzhou, Jiaxing, Huzhou, Ningbo, Shaoxing, Wenzhou, Taizhou, Quzhou, and Yan'an to guide the reorganization of various merchant groups according to law.

The Hangzhou City Merchant Organization Unification Committee held a general membership registration, scheduled to begin on July 1. Yesterday, the general registration method was submitted to the Municipal Government for verification.

The price of rice at the Hushen rice market has soared in the past week, increasing by two yuan per picul. Saigon rice has also risen accordingly. However, it was decided during the last price increase for retail rice that prices would not be discussed until July 10, so the original price is temporarily maintained. However, due to excessive losses, the rice color of each vendor has changed, and the price of 14 yuan per picul has no goods available.

Local Correspondence

Jiading

The long-distance telephone will soon be completed. The County Construction Bureau handled the long-distance telephone project, which was originally scheduled to be completed by the end of June. The lines in the western townships have already been installed. However, in Fangtai and Huangdu, disputes arose over the location of the generator installation, so the lines have not been installed and communication is not possible. All lines in the southern townships have been connected, except for the section between Nanxiang and Jiwang, where the installation of underwater cables has not been completed due to obstacles caused by ships traveling in the Wusong River. The Jia-Cao line and Jia-Guang line in the eastern townships have already been installed. Generators have been installed in Xuhang, Caowang, Chengqiao, Jianbang, Guangfu, and other places. Communication was established yesterday.

Robbery in Three Small Villages: The residents of the Three Small Villages west of Nanxiang Town consist of only four or five households. The family of a certain surname is quite wealthy. At about 9 p.m. on the 25th, a bandit ship suddenly arrived and anchored near the village. More than twenty bandits, speaking the Jiangbei dialect, with towels wrapped around their heads and carrying iron rulers and bayonets, broke into houses and robbed them for more than an hour before leaving. They robbed more than four hundred and fifty silver dollars, sixty thousand copper coins, more than ten piculs of white rice, and clothes, etc., worth about six to seven hundred yuan, totaling a loss of more than one thousand yuan.

Kunshan

Innocent Merchants and Citizens Detained: Zhou Yinlin, who runs a teahouse in Zhangpu Town, was suddenly arrested yesterday by Wen, the Inspector of the County Public Security Bureau, along with a dozen members of the debt-collecting team armed with guns. Without asking for any explanation, Zhou was arrested and taken to the bureau. It was later learned that the reason for the arrest was that someone had anonymously reported that Zhou was involved in collusion with bandits. After interrogation, there was no evidence, and it was found that he had been falsely accused. He was released on bail. A piece of anonymous letter has caused such an ordeal, truly an injustice.

The Director of the Construction Bureau is Accused: Wu Junyu, the Director of the Construction Bureau of this county, has been in Kunshan for two years and has made no achievements in various construction projects. The construction of the Kun-Tai Road has been suspended for half a year, and there has been no report on income and expenditure, causing dissatisfaction among all circles. It is now heard that the County Party Affairs Consolidation Committee has requested the Provincial Government to order the Construction Department to send personnel to thoroughly investigate. Songjiang

Three Bandits Executed by Firing Squad: Pan Jingqing, the local security officer of Xiaozheng, was evil and tyrannical, recruiting bandits and engaging in robbery and looting. He secretly sat and divided the spoils, committing crimes in Qingpu within this territory. After the incident, he was arrested, and accomplices Wang Jingqin and Liu Xiaomei were also captured. After interrogation, their crimes were confirmed, and they were sentenced to death according to law. The Provincial Government approved the execution by telegram. Upon receiving the telegram, the County Government dispatched police to bring Pan, Wang, and Liu to justice, verified their identities, and took them to the Yuhuang Pavilion execution ground to be executed by firing squad.

Cooperative Movement and Pest Control Measures: Yesterday, the County Government convened a meeting of representatives from various agencies to prepare for the cooperative movement and pest control movement. Ge Hongye from the Provincial Insect Bureau attended the meeting. County Magistrate Jin, as the chairman, reported the provincial order that the cooperative movement should be held starting from the first Saturday of July this year (World Cooperative Day). He also reported the order from the Agricultural Department that the Provincial Insect Bureau had submitted a plan for the first pest control propaganda campaign in the province. After deliberation by the Provincial Government, it was ordered to hold county propaganda meetings and township patrols from July 3 to July 17. The result of the discussion was to combine the preparations for the two movements and hold them separately, using the Public Library as the venue. The publicity fee for the cooperative movement was set at sixty yuan, and the County Party Department, Farmers Bank, and People's Education Center were designated to preside over the cooperative movement. The Education Bureau, County Farm, Agricultural Education Center, and Provincial Suili Experimental Farm were designated to preside over the pest control section, and the general affairs and propaganda sections were separately prepared.

Summary of the Meeting of Village Chiefs: The County Government convened a meeting of village chiefs from various districts under the county on the 28th. County Magistrate Jin, as the chairman, reported on important cases and then resolved that the county's previous administrative meeting had decided to start a household registration donation to supplement the police recruitment. The Provincial Government approved the change of the name of the household registration donation to defense donation, and the method of donating money according to the previous divisions was slightly changed to show consideration for the people's difficulties. A manual survey will be conducted by local people recommended by the district chiefs and hired by the county to assist the district chiefs in the survey to facilitate the handling. The provincial order that officials and autonomous staff must take an oath must be reported before July 15 for compilation. Some district chiefs proposed to prohibit fish nests and crab trapping, and it was resolved that the county would issue a notice to prohibit it. After the discussion, the administrative expenses for each district were issued, and the meeting adjourned.

The First District Office Prepares for Price Stabilization: As the period for price stabilization is approaching, the First District Office convened a price stabilization meeting yesterday and decided to purchase No. 2 Xian tribute rice. The Rice Industry Association was entrusted to order it and transport 1,000 bags to Songjiang before July 15, and the rest will be transported to Songjiang in batches. The boundaries of each branch office will be divided to avoid confusion. After the rice arrives, the branches will take the receipts to the district office to collect it. The expenses for each branch office will be submitted to the county government for approval, as the first district has no surplus funds.

Fengxian

Relief Measures After the Hail Disaster: Since this county suffered a hail and drought disaster, the County Government immediately convened a local meeting to discuss relief and has already decided on ten measures, the most important of which are: (1) Order the district offices in the disaster-stricken areas to accurately register the number of damaged fields and the names of the deceased. (2) Landlords should lend seven corners of planting capital per picul to tenants so that they can purchase seeds and replant. Families with less than fifteen mu of self-cultivated land and the poor should have their district offices borrow seeds from shops and repay them after the autumn harvest. (3) Issue a notice to all land and rice shops that they must not raise the price of seeds, and those who violate this will be severely punished.

Cleaning Up Arrears in Land Tax: Hong, the former county magistrate, convened a committee of various agencies to clean up arrears in land tax, but it was suspended halfway, so it did not proceed. Now, County Magistrate Shen Qingchen believes that the amount of arrears in land tax is huge, which not only affects the tax revenue of the national and provincial treasuries, but also greatly affects local undertakings that should respond to the surtax. Therefore, he advocates thorough cleanup and has reorganized the committee and hired a certain Zhang as the person in charge, limited to two months to make a roster and investigate.

The Kidnapping of the Lu Family Has Not Yet Been Resolved: In Fang Sixteen Tu near Zhuanghang, a nine-year-old child from the wealthy Lu family was kidnapped. After receiving a letter from the bandits demanding a ransom of 20,000 yuan, the mother went to a certain place on the agreed date to prepare to negotiate, but no one came after waiting all day. At the same time, Ding Zhiyan, the captain of the police team in this county, heard about this situation and sent squad leader Yang Xingsheng to track it down for strict investigation. According to the report, the victim is still in the countryside, and he has joined forces with Wang Jinchuan, the captain of the water police team, to search in separate directions in order to arrest the bandits. Although the Lu family is nominally said to have three families combined, the family property is less than one hundred mu, and it has long been exhausted after two robberies. The mother cannot cope with it and has repeatedly wanted to commit suicide. The misery of the bandits is truly heartbreaking.

Wuxi

The Silk Industry Association Scheduled a Meeting: Since the beginning of summer, the weather in this county has been abnormal, resulting in the death of many summer silkworms in the four townships. It is said that only two or three out of ten silkworms survived compared to previous years, which is a great misfortune for farmers. It is now heard that Hua Shaochun and others, the executive members of the Silk Industry Association, have decided to convene a meeting of all committee members at 2 p.m. on July 1 to discuss the opening date of the market and the price of fresh silkworms, as the summer silkworms are about to be placed on the cocooning frame.

The Labor-Capital Problem in Silk Factories Has Not Been Resolved: The Labor Union of Silk Factory Workers in this county previously proposed twenty-four labor-capital conditions, which were approved and signed by the Silk Factory Industry Association. Unexpectedly, the capital suddenly repented at the expiration date, which caused disputes. It is learned that only a few factory owners opposed this matter, resulting in internal inconsistency. Yesterday afternoon, the Labor Union held its 34th committee meeting and resolved the following matters: (1) Adopt a calm attitude and urge the Party and government agencies to resolve the matter fairly as soon as possible. (2) Draft and print a declaration for distribution. (3) Order all members to abide by the association's discipline and wait for a resolution, and not to take any out-of-line actions, and instruct the sub-labor unions to comply and be responsible for conveying the instructions to all members. After the meeting, the executive committee members Tao Shensheng, Hua Nianzhu, Ye Qiaoyun, etc., went to the county government to meet with County Magistrate Sun to ask for instructions. County Magistrate Sun expressed that he would be responsible for convening a meeting of both labor and capital to mediate within a short period of time. Tao and others were satisfied and left.

Military Police Salary Stolen: Wang Longdao, the company commander of the Eighth Company of the First Regiment of Military Police stationed in Chengjiang, came to Wuxi a few days ago to receive more than 1,300 yuan from the regimental headquarters and placed it in a handbag. That night, he took the Cheng-Xi ferry back to Chengjiang. When he arrived, it was after 10 p.m. Wang walked back to the camp alone, carrying the handbag and a flashlight. When he passed through the dark area near the Wenchang Temple Stone Horse Lane outside the East Gate of Chengjiang, three people wearing black clothes suddenly came forward to rob him. Wang was pushed into a rice field by the roadside, and the salary and official documents in the handbag were taken away. When he climbed out of the rice field, the bandits were long gone. He immediately rushed to the Longgang company headquarters and sent a team to search everywhere, and reported to the county government and the regimental headquarters in Wuxi to request a joint search.

Sun Junxi was Escorted Back to Wuxi: Sun Junxi, the former Minister of Propaganda of the County Party Department, was arrested for gambling and suspected of counter-revolutionary activities and sent to Suzhou for trial by the High Court. The counter-revolutionary part was sentenced to six months in prison, which has now expired. However, the case of Tan Qixuan, the director of the Beishang Township Administration Bureau in Wuxi, who was killed, is still under investigation. Tan Zhongying, the father of the deceased, has accused Sun and Lu Wugao, who is in custody, in the county. Therefore, the County Government yesterday specially sent political police Liu Yirong and Wu Rongsheng to Suzhou with documents to escort Sun back. Tang Yiqin, a member of the backlog clearance case, opened a court for trial. Sun confessed that Lu Shigao shot and killed Tan Qixuan, and that he had reported the case, so Lu framed him out of hatred. Tang interrogated him briefly and ordered him to be sent to the detention center for custody, pending the trial of Lu Shigao for verification.

Changzhou

News After the Counter-Revolutionary Suspect was Sent to Beijing: The military police stationed in Changzhou previously found anti-revolutionary language in the diary of Xiong Jihuan, the deputy head of Bajiao Township, in the Jiqing Hotel. The witnesses were also taken to the company headquarters and transferred to the regimental headquarters of the First Regiment in the capital for interrogation. Xiong Jihuan confessed that the anti-revolutionary words were framed by He Wenquan and Wu Jinkun, who had a feud with him. According to the confession, the regimental headquarters sent a team to Changzhou to join the Benniu Public Security Second Branch to arrest He and Wu and send them to Beijing for interrogation with Xiong. Yesterday, the district chief Song Zhen requested the county government to release He and others, stating that He and others had been acting properly and serving as primary school teachers with enthusiasm for school affairs. District Chief Song then submitted a document to the county for verification.

A 108-Year-Old Man Came to Zhenjiang: Li Shangyi, a 108-year-old man, a native of Henan, came to Zhenjiang on his way from Shanghai to visit places in passing, believing in Islam. Before the age of seventy-five, Mr. Li had visited Zhenjiang before. The local Islamic followers in Zhenjiang believe that the old man is strong and healthy, a blessing among people, and has a strong faith in Islam. Therefore, after he checked in, many men and women came to visit him. It is heard that Mr. Li plans to visit various agencies and scenic spots. Inspection of Stamps Caused Disputes: The Money Industry Association has recently received letters from various money houses stating that inspectors from the Stamp Tax Bureau inspect stamps and go to various houses to search in groups of three to five without the company of gang police, harassing them at will. If there is no missing stamp, they forcibly sell stamps, up to several hundred yuan. If their wishes are not fulfilled, they take the opportunity to search, turning over boxes and cabinets, and nitpicking. The money houses have a large turnover of silver dollars every day. For safety, they would rather stop business than allow them to trample and suffer unexpected losses. Jiangsu Province's Disaster Relief Progress: The Jiangsu Province Disaster Relief Association held its eleventh meeting at the Civil Affairs Department at 4 p.m. yesterday. Cheng Jingsheng, Lu Xiaobo, and six others attended. Chairman Hu Pu'an resolved the following matters: (1) Allocate disaster relief funds to various counties: (1) Siyang and Lianshui will each receive 2,000 yuan, and Suqian will receive 10,000 yuan. (2) Gaoyou will receive an additional 1,000 yuan, Huaiyin will receive an additional 2,400 yuan, Yixing will receive an additional 2,600 yuan, Zhenjiang will receive an additional 500 yuan, and Yancheng will receive an additional 2,500 yuan. (3) The funds to be allocated will be fully distributed by the Temporary Relief Association from the 20,000 yuan allocated by the Finance Department, and the shortage will be temporarily paid by the Relief Association, and then returned to the Finance Department after the Finance Department allocates funds again. (1) The association will send another letter to the Finance Department requesting the continued allocation of 10,000 yuan to aid in disaster relief.

Qingjiang

A Bandit from Shuyang Arrested: Zhu Lianfang, the captain of the Huaiyin Police Brigade, recently received a report from detective Li Yunpeng that Tang Wenxiang, a notorious bandit from Shuyang, Haizhou, had moved to No. 40 Wuliuqiao, Donghou Street, South Gate of the city. According to the report, Zhu led five police officers to arrest Tang at 9 p.m. on the 23rd and took him to the brigade for interrogation. Tang confessed that he was thirty-five years old, a native of Haizhou, and that he had found the residence through Liu Bingsheng on the 2nd of this month. He had committed many crimes in Shuyang when he was young, but had never been caught. He said that his arrest this time was perhaps due to the will of heaven. According to Liu Bingsheng, he knew Tang in prison before, and he helped him find a house because Tang entrusted him to do so. The address of No. 40 Wuliuqiao is true. After the confession, Zhu regarded the case as a bandit case and sent Tang and Liu to the county government on the morning of the 24th.

Gaoyou

The Robbery and Burning of Lujiabao: Guo, a merchant in Lujiabao, which belongs to the county, opened the Zhentai Grocery Store, which was doing well. Unexpectedly, seven bandits suddenly came at about 3 p.m. the other day, each holding guns, and rushed into the house, overturning boxes and cabinets. They only found more than one hundred silver dollars. The bandits were still not satisfied and demanded a huge sum of money from Guo, but failed. They then dispersed to the four corners of the house and set it on fire. In an instant, the fire was raging, burning dozens of tiled houses, thousands of bags of flour, and hundreds of vats of bean oil, with losses of about tens of thousands of yuan. Guo has now gone to the county to report the case.

Nantong

The Bandits' Night Attack on Shigang Failed: On the night of the 26th, a large group of bandits suddenly arrived in Shigang City, Beixiang, Tongyi, intending to attack and rob it. The security forces surrounded and intercepted them. Knowing that there were preparations, the bandits immediately retreated.

Opium Traffickers Are Active Again: The voices of official investigations against opium traffickers in Tongyi have recently subsided, and they are now active again. The Yaogang Poyang ship unloaded a large amount of opium pills upon arrival in the port. It is heard that a protection fee of three yuan per package is paid, causing a public outcry. The Phoenix Bridge Bandits' Riot: On the morning of the 27th, three hundred bandits from Haimen County rioted in the Phoenix Bridge area in the east of Nantong. The provincial police team stationed in Qidong rushed to suppress them.

The County Court President Was Accused: Dong Banggan, the president and judge of the Nantong County Court, was accused of失態and漫駡by lawyer Jiang Jue and others to the High Court. The High Court ordered the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor to come to Tong to investigate. Pinghu

Tai Bao A Shu's Henchman, Monk Wang, Was Arrested: Tai Bao Ajin's henchman, Monk Wang, lived in Luwan Temple and was a neighbor of the notorious bandit Zhu Luo A Mei. Wang joined the robbery cases in Yaqian and Xincang last winter and this spring. Recently, seeing that the provincial defense forces were strictly arresting bandits in the eastern townships, he fled to Zhapu on the other day and temporarily lived in Jiang Along's house in Beimen as a farmhand. On the afternoon of the 25th, Shen Asi, a temporary detective of the County Government's patrol team, learned about it and immediately telegraphed Captain Yang. Captain Yang telegraphed Duonmu, the branch director of the Zhapu Public Security Bureau, asking him to send police to assist in the arrest. According to Wang Hesheng, he admitted to robbing Xincang with a knife this spring. Ningbo

Summary of Banditry: Zhou, a resident of Zhou Village in Changshou District, Fenghua, was not wealthy, but he was also coveted by bandits. On the night of the 24th, six bandits suddenly came with wooden shell guns and flashlights, broke into the house, and tied up Zhou's son, demanding a ransom of 3,000 yuan. The family is now having difficulty raising the money and is very anxious. Also, the home of Wu Jialin, the village chief of Liu Fu Village, was entered by five bandits at about 9 p.m. the other night, asking Wu for 500 yuan in travel expenses. As a result, they extorted 40 silver dollars. Also, the Sanchakou Village in Shuanghui Township, Yuyao, is located in a remote mountain area, and the bandit forces are rampant, coming and going without avoiding anyone. At 7 p.m. on the 24th, more than ten bandits wearing blue cloth short clothes were found again. Five of them were buying snacks at the Wannian Tea Pavilion, three were hiding under the tree shed, and three were detouring in the village. Wei, a villager, saw that their behavior was suspicious and immediately notified the villagers to hold weapons for defense. Fortunately, they were not robbed.

Yin-Feng Highway Collects and Transports Mail: Since the opening of the Yin-Feng Automobile Road of the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau, business has been quite prosperous. Now, in order to develop its business, it has contacted the post office to collect and transport Yin-Feng mail. Yin-Feng mail used to be delivered by small boats and had to arrive the next day, which was very inconvenient. Since the change to using cars to transport it on the 9th of this month, it can be reached on the same day. The bridge can send mail to Yong with 1 hour, which is faster. Since the implementation of this method, both the road bureau and the post office have been able to increase their income, and the people feel more convenient. However, heavy mail (i.e., newspapers, packages, etc.) is still delivered by small boats.

Shaoxing

Price Stabilization Implemented: The Shaoxing Food Maintenance Association will handle the price stabilization of 13,000 bags of rice, which have now been loaded and transported to Shaoxing. It is scheduled to open at 14 yuan per picul. Because it is necessary to consume 50,000 yuan according to cost calculation, it has been sent to the county and reported to the province for record, and the loss will be withdrawn from the reserve donation.

Cooperative Movement Propaganda: All party and government agencies in Shaoxing were ordered to organize a preparatory committee for the cooperative movement propaganda week. The first meeting was held at the county department on the 27th, and Chairman Zhang Jixiao decided to hold the opening ceremony on July 5. Representatives of the county party department, the Construction Bureau, and the county chamber of commerce were appointed as standing committee members. The Chamber of Commerce refused to take on the general affairs section, so the county party department took on the editing section and the Construction Bureau took on the guidance section. On July 1, a representative conference of various agencies and groups will be convened to discuss the progress of the matter. Tragedy of Broken Power Pole: Since the installation of the new machine, the Daming Electric Light Company has been replacing the power poles along the street these days. At about 4 p.m. yesterday, while working on Huajiao, the power pole suddenly broke due to years of decay, pulling down several poles. Two mechanics fell down and injured a child selling peaches there. Except for one person who was slightly injured, the other two were bleeding profusely and unconscious. They were immediately taken to the hospital for treatment.

Bombs Exploded and Were Seized and Sent to the County: On the 24th, in Xiaoshan Dongxiang Xiaosihuan, three soldiers in military uniforms, Liu Guozhen, Liu Pengfei, and Wang Agou, were carrying three bombs on the road. Suining

Shijiadun Weizi Was Robbed Again: Since this spring, Wei San and Liu Rongduo, well-known bandits in Suining, have been rampant in the three counties of Suining, Suqian, and Si. In Suining County alone, there have been five or sixty cases of mining weizi walls being架. The number of households being taken is even more uncounted. Recently, the Shijiadun Weizi, more than ten li east of the county, was broken by the bandits led by Wei and Liu, and they occupied Zhang Weizi on the 22nd. The momentum was quite large, and the encirclement team did not dare to advance to suppress them. According to reports, the Weizi was attacked by Liu's bandits once before, and all the houses in the Weizi were burned down, and more than 800 people were killed. Afterwards, the Jiangsu Provincial Government provided disaster relief funds, and the Agricultural and Mining Department constructed new villages. Unexpectedly, the new villages are still under construction, and they have suffered another catastrophe. Twenty or forty residents were killed, and the houses in the Weizi were completely burned. The grains, grass, clothing, and belongings were all lost. All the wood purchased by the Agricultural and Mining Department for the construction of the new villages was also burned. All the weizi walls that have not been captured are now in danger.

Letter

Letter from the Suqian County Public Security Bureau 12

Respected Editor,

Regarding the news reported in your newspaper on June 19 that the Suqian Public Security Bureau was accused, according to the investigation, the monk Xiangzhai Jisheng and others of Jile Temple Wu Hua Ding, Suqian, led the knife club to attack the city last year and have been publicly wanted and the temple property has been confiscated. Previously, according to the Provincial Committee, the county estimated the temple property and divided it into four shares for the temple and the remaining six shares for local public welfare. On the morning of the 8th, the county notified the monks of the temple to comply. Unexpectedly, the monk Xiangzhai felt angry and厭世at the sudden division of the fields passed down from his ancestor's cassock, and secretly swallowed a wooden fish. On the afternoon of that day, Chen Jianming, an inspector from the Civil Affairs Department, and Committee Member Wang from the County Party Department went to our bureau and ordered us to send police to arrest the monks Xiangzhai and Jisheng to the bureau. Inspector Chen interrogated them briefly and learned that Xiangzhai had swallowed gold, so he sent him to the hospital for treatment and sent Jisheng to the county for custody. (Xiangzhai Zhitun Jin was released on the 16th.) He was also sent to the county for custody. The monk did not understand the truth and sent a telegram without authorization to arrest and frighten him. The facts that monk Xiangzhai was forced to swallow gold and monk Jisheng was frightened and fainted are not true. Therefore, we specially write to request correction to avoid confusing the hearing. I am grateful. Suqian County Public Security Bureau, June 24.

Local News

Today's Conference Of 13

Industrial and Commercial Management Association

Time: 3 PM

Location: Bankers Association

The Chinese Industrial and Commercial Management Association is scheduled to hold its inaugural meeting at the Bankers Association, No. 4 Hong Kong Road, at 3 PM today. Minister of Industry and Commerce, Mr. Kong Xiangxi, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday specifically to attend today's meeting. The key information about the association is compiled and reported below:

The Preparatory Committee held a meeting yesterday at 6 PM at the Bankers Club regarding the preparatory work for the general assembly. The five committee members present were Liu Hongsheng, Lu Feibo Hong, Pan Xulun, Qian Chengxu, and Shou Jingwei. The results of their discussions are as follows: (1) Committee member Liu Zhanen and Committee member Hu Shuhua proposed that the association's name be determined as the Chinese Industrial and Commercial Scientific Management Association. It was resolved to submit this proposal to the general assembly for a decision. (2) The report on the preparatory process was resolved to be revised, passed, and submitted to the general assembly for reporting by the chairman of the Preparatory Committee, Mr. Mu Ouchu. (3) The agenda for the general assembly was scheduled. (4) All received proposals and opinions were sorted separately and submitted to the general assembly for discussion.

I then convened a meeting to draft the articles of association and scheduled the inaugural meeting for June 29th. This will be fortunate for the association and fortunate for the future of enterprises.

Customs Duty on Ship Tonnage at Tianjin 14

Must be pre-collected at Shanghai Customs

To be handled according to the Ministry of Finance's order

Since the National Government ordered the sealing of Tianjin Customs, the volume of goods transported from Shanghai to Tianjin has also slightly decreased. Yesterday, it was learned that Shanghai Customs received an order from the Ministry of Finance stating that the ship tonnage duties payable by ships importing into Tianjin Customs must also be prepaid at Shanghai Customs. Foreign merchant shipping companies, fearing that Tianjin Customs might still forcibly collect these tonnage duties, have been presenting requests to their consular corps for instructions on how to proceed. The consular corps stated that this case had already been telegraphed to their respective governments for instructions, and they were awaiting a response and would observe the situation for the time being.

Silver Market Gradually Improving 15

Due to Foreign Banks Shipping Silver for Export

The price of silver in the local market has slightly improved recently, rising slightly compared to the lowest point. Yesterday, the lowest price for silver reached 576 taels. Although there is no hope of completely recovering silver prices at the moment, it may not continue to plummet. According to a survey in banking circles yesterday, one of the reasons is said to be that foreign banks have not been secretly shipping in much silver recently, and because foreign banks have too much silver in storage, the market price has fallen below that of foreign countries, so they are shipping large amounts of raw silver overseas to various countries to find ways to sell it. As a result, the storage amount is gradually decreasing, and the market price can be maintained in its original state.

Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company 16

After Passing the Bidding Sale

Both Officials and Civilians Have Serious Concerns

The Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company has officially passed the proposal to sell the bid to the International Company and will soon implement the transfer in accordance with the regulations. Various groups and citizens in our country are extremely indignant upon hearing this. According to investigations yesterday, the Ministry of Communications and various public groups have long known that the concession authorities and the company have had this plan for a long time and have already determined the methods. Therefore, they already knew that it must be passed. However, only a few Chinese shareholders attended the meeting that day, and some Westerners also opposed this proposal, which shows the sentiment of the people. Therefore, the National Government has decided to go a step further and will formally lodge a strong protest with the consular corps in Shanghai through diplomatic channels, urging them to urge the Public Works Department authorities not to formally approve the sale in order to remedy the situation. The most relevant groups in the special district, such as the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Citizens' Union, the Chinese Taxpayers Association, and the Users' Union, have joined forces and are gathering the strength of various groups to take the second step of resistance, urging the purchaser, International Company, to realize the situation and voluntarily give up the purchase. Otherwise, they will take passive resistance to protect sovereignty. They are currently in contact with each other and will express their views soon.

Chinese Users Issued a Declaration Yesterday

The Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company Chinese Users' Union convened a meeting at 2 PM yesterday and resolved the following: (1) Issue a declaration to awaken all groups in the city to provide united assistance. (2) Telegraph the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Communications to file a strong protest and declare that the International Telegraph and Telephone Company has no right to operate telephone services in Chinese territory. (3) Warn the International Telegraph and Telephone Company that all Chinese users cannot violate national laws and cooperate with the company before formally obtaining an exclusive franchise from the Chinese government. (4) Telegraph the American Minister to China, Johnson, to protest, and telegraph our Minister to the United States, Wu Chaoshu, to appeal to the US government to protest. The telegram stated that the International Telegraph and Telephone Company has not obtained an exclusive franchise in China. The meeting adjourned after the resolution. The declaration is recorded below:

Our country's telegraph and telephone industry is state-owned, as determined by Article 2 of the Telecommunications Regulations promulgated by the government on April 18, 1915. Private telephone services are not allowed to operate in a certain area without government permission. Article 3 of the same regulations also has clear provisions. Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, the state ownership of telegraphs and telephones has not changed, and private telephone services still need to be approved by the government. The approval of this private telephone service is not unique to our country; all countries in the world are the same. Therefore, those who operate telephone services in our country's territory should respect and abide by our country's laws and sovereignty. Previously, the Ministry of Communications believed that the telephone services operated by the Shanghai Telephone Company were not effective enough, and it was planned to recover the business by the Ministry at a price or approve private operation in order to improve the efficiency of public utilities. However, the Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Telephone Company did not pay attention to the above points and openly held a meeting and decided to sell the business to the International Telegraph and Telephone Company when the Chinese shareholders generally did not attend. The International Telegraph and Telephone Company also did not pay attention to the above points and rashly bid to buy this act that disregards our country's laws and sovereignty, which cannot be tolerated by any people or any country, and is especially heartbreaking for all our users. Now all our users have made up their minds, in addition to requesting the government to lodge a protest and declare that the telephone services operated by the International Telegraph and Telephone Company violate our country's laws and have not been approved by the government, we should take effective measures to stop its illegal business and absolutely prepare not to use illegal telephones and not to cooperate with the International Telegraph and Telephone Company. We will do what we say and will not regret our decision. We hope that all sectors will provide assistance to maintain national laws and sovereignty. This declaration is hereby issued for your consideration.

Treacherous Merchants Manipulating the Rice Market 17

Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs Strictly Investigating Under Orders

Recently, the Municipal Government learned that treacherous merchants have been manipulating the rice market. In addition to issuing a strict ban, it instructed the Bureau of Social Affairs yesterday: "According to reports, the price of rice in this city has risen continuously in recent days, with the highest price exceeding 20 yuan per stone. This is unprecedented. After investigation, the price increase is not due to a shortage of rice, but is caused by a small number of treacherous merchants manipulating the market for their own selfish gain, disregarding the people's food supply. This is a scourge of society and is extremely hateful. It is necessary to thoroughly investigate and severely punish them as a warning to others. In addition to ordering the Public Security Bureau to issue a notice, you are hereby ordered to immediately conduct a thorough investigation and punish them without any consideration. Also, inform the Rice Price Evaluation Committee to actively proceed and report the handling situation at any time for inspection. This order is of utmost importance."

Future Rice Price Settlement 18

The Bureau of Social Affairs Scheduled a Meeting

The Municipal Grain Association has determined that there are many disputes over future rice contracts among merchants. Therefore, the settlement cannot be used as a solution, and once a bad example is set, it will cause endless troubles. It is reported that the Bureau of Social Affairs has scheduled a meeting of the two organizations for July 2 to discuss and resolve the matter.

New Method for Collecting Taxes at Tianjin Customs 19

The Xinfeng Steamer Will Go to Tianjin on Tuesday

Regarding the suspension of customs inspection of imported goods at Tianjin Customs, the British and Japanese consuls in Shanghai have proposed discussions and plan to send personnel to Tianjin to negotiate a solution. Yesterday, the local Beiyang gang received a telegram from Tianjin stating that for goods shipped from Shanghai to Tianjin, if half of the Tianjin Customs duty has been paid in Shanghai, Tianjin Customs will still require the cargo owner to pay the duty upon arrival in Tianjin. However, in order to protect the interests of the cargo owner and avoid additional losses, Tianjin Customs has agreed to issue a tax receipt, and the cargo owner can hold this tax receipt to request a refund of the half-tax paid from Shanghai Customs. It would be best if the Jianghai Customs could refund the money. Otherwise, Tianjin Customs only needs to obtain proof that the cargo owner has indeed not recovered the half-tax paid, and it can use the receipt to collect the money in Tianjin.

However, regardless of whether the tax has been paid or not, it must be paid in full when the goods arrive in Tianjin.

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xinfeng steamer returned to Shanghai from Tianjin yesterday and will still need to open to Tianjin on Tuesday, because there are still some goods in Shanghai that need to be trial-shipped to Tianjin to meet the needs.

After Public Evaluation 24

Rice Shops Still Collect Commission

Yesterday, reporters from various newspapers saw a report stating that since the Bureau of Social Affairs held the North City rice boat registration and ordered the Rice Shop Association to evaluate the rice for sale, the North Zhabei rice shops had ceased operations because the rice was evaluated and sold directly by the association to the Jia Gengtang for distribution to various shops, without going through the rice shops. They asked a Mr. from the Bureau of Social Affairs about this matter. According to him, the boats arriving at the riverbanks in North City are sold to the evaluation office by the original merchants, and the Doumi Industry Association designates the rice shops in North City to evaluate the rice in turn and collect commissions as before, which are fairly distributed to all merchants in the same industry. The original interests of the rice shop merchants are not lost, but the operating method has changed from dispersion to concentration. This is a temporary management method during a rice shortage. Once the rice price falls back to a considerable level, it will be revoked. As for the saying that business is slack, it is naturally rare for boats to arrive during this time of the year when the old rice has been consumed and the new rice has not yet been harvested. This is probably just a small number.

The propaganda of a few people with ulterior motives is not credible. Mr. also stated that the local rice merchants have also suddenly realized that they will evaluate and sell the rice according to the evaluation and will no longer wait and see, hoping that all parties will work together to overcome this difficulty and wait for the new rice to be harvested. This is fortunate for the people of this city.
