Zhenhua Girls' School in Suzhou Holds Graduation Ceremony Yesterday 64

Yesterday, the 28th, Zhenhua Girls' School in Suzhou held its graduation ceremony. At 9 AM, despite the humid heat, guests arrived, including leaders and representatives from various institutions and schools, school directors Zhang Zhongren, Zhang Yunbo, Liu Beimu, Bei Zaian, Xu Boming, and prominent figures from the education sector, such as Yang Xingfo. After the customary opening remarks, the school directors and principal presented their reports. Yang Xingfo gave a speech titled "The Psychology that Chinese Women Should Transform." He emphasized (1) focusing on revolutionary work as individuals, rather than being confined to the traditional concept of "virtuous wife and good mother"; (2) expanding the concept of aesthetics to include endeavors in art, hygiene, science, and literature; (3) extending their influence to the entire society and community; and (4) applying scientific methods to improve women's lives. His words were extremely insightful. Afterwards, the Party representative, Yang Zu, delivered a closing speech, praising the school as the cultural center of Suzhou. The county government representative and Director of Education of Wu County, Wu Guanghan, also gave speeches. Director Wu stated that the county's annual education budget was 500,000 yuan, but there was a lack of girls' middle schools. The school filled a significant gap in society. The principal of the girls' middle school, Chen She, the vocational school principal, Pan Jianqing, and Zhang Yunbo and Xu Boming also gave speeches. The head of the school, Shen Jiying, gave a farewell speech, encouraging the students to embrace the qualities of "action," "tranquility," "responsibility," and "detachment." The ceremony concluded with the presentation of awards and music.

Qixia Rural Teachers College to Hold Graduation Ceremony 65

Qixia Rural Teachers College has gained quite a reputation in the past two years. Recently, the school's new student enrollment examination attracted over 600 applicants from as many as 38 counties. Within Jiangnan, Wujin County had the most applicants, followed by Jiangning and Zhenjiang. In Jiangbei, Taixing County had the most applicants, followed by Jiangdu and Liuhe. Female students account for approximately 8% of the total. The current graduating class consists of thirty-seven students who have now completed their studies and are scheduled to hold a graduation ceremony on July 1st. The graduates come from fourteen counties, with Jurong having the most. Local News

City Education Bureau Thoroughly Investigates Extortion of Graduation Certificate Fees 66

According to regulations, graduation certificates for primary and secondary schools in the city must be purchased from the City Education Bureau. Each certificate costs only one dime (yuan) for printing fees. Secondary school certificates also require a three-dime stamp, while primary school certificates are exempt. This procedure is intended to standardize certificates. However, it has recently been reported that some school authorities are privately demanding certificate fees ranging from two to four yuan from graduates, threatening to withhold the certificates if the fee is not paid. The City Education Bureau considers such behavior to be extortion and has dispatched personnel to conduct a thorough investigation.

National Arithmetic Exhibition Results Returned, Exhibition Extended 67

The City Education Bureau issued a notice yesterday stating that the National Language and Arithmetic Exhibition was originally scheduled to close on June 29th, with schools sending representatives to retrieve their exhibits starting June 30th. However, due to the large number of exhibits and the time required for judging, the judging will not be completed until June 30th. Therefore, the date for schools to retrieve their exhibits has been rescheduled to start on July 1st.

News of the City Elementary School Joint Examination 68

The results of the graduation joint examination have been determined. This year, 111 municipal and registered private schools participated in the elementary school graduation joint examination, with 2,390 students taking the examination. 1,816 students passed, and 574 failed. The top three students with the best results, who will be awarded certificates, are graduates from Shanghai Private Elementary School, Tonghui Private Elementary School, and the affiliated elementary school of Jingye Municipal Middle School.

Order to Send Graduation Photos: The City Education Bureau's elementary school graduation joint examination this year is an unprecedented event. Therefore, a group photo should be taken to commemorate it. However, due to the large number of students, there is a lack of suitable open space for gathering. Therefore, each school is specifically ordered to take a 2.5-inch portrait photo of each graduate and submit them to the Bureau by a deadline for compilation into a booklet.

After the Ministry of Education suspended enrollment at Labor University, all the students of the school hosted reporters from local newspapers at the Sichuan Road YMCA yesterday afternoon to report on the incident and clarify the truth to labor union members. The reporters responded by saying they would uphold a fair attitude and vigorously assist.

St. John's 51st Graduation Ceremony 70

St. John's University held its 51st graduation ceremony yesterday afternoon at 4 p.m. After the ceremony, President Bu delivered the opening remarks. Acting Academic Dean Zhao Xiuhong gave a report, stating that it was a great honor and pleasure to welcome the guests to the 51st graduation ceremony. He then briefly reported on the events of the academic year. The biggest event of the academic year was the celebration of the school's 50th anniversary in mid-December last year, along with the opening ceremony of the student activity center. Today's graduation ceremony is being held in this auditorium for the first time. This year, there are 573 university and high school students, a significant increase from last year. The number of faculty members is the same as in previous years, with the exception of the unfortunate passing of French teacher Ms. Lambert. Ms. Lambert had taught at the school for many years, and her passing is deeply mourned. This year, two professors were sent to the school by the Carnegie Endowment for International Peace, one being Dr. Martin, a professor of political science at the University of Washington in Seattle, who lectured on [Modern Political Trends] in mid-December last year, and the other being Dr. Teqiu, a history professor at Whistling University in Natic Province, who lectured on [The Foundation of International Order] in March. The medical school is thriving this year, with 24 students in the first year, the largest number in its history. There are also 13 students planning to enter the medical school in the second half of the year. China desperately needs highly trained doctors, but the medical school's expenses are very high. The school has received donations from the American Board of Trustees and other sources, allowing it to continue operating. In May, Mr. Hua Chi, the director-general sent by the school's founder, came to China to investigate the problems that church schools need to solve. During this academic year, Academic Dean and Acting Vice President Shen Siliang traveled to the United States and will return to the school in the second half of the year. After the school was temporarily suspended in 1927, there were very few senior students in the College of Arts and Sciences. Today, 43 high school students, 24 students from the College of Arts and Sciences, 1 graduate student, and 14 medical students are graduating. One special thing about the graduates is that there is a chef who also earned a Bachelor of Arts degree, the first person in China to do so. Cao Yunxiang delivered a speech on [The Benefits and Responsibilities of Great Universities].

The Photoreproduction of the Hundred Naps Edition of the Twenty-Four Histories 74

The Twenty-Four Histories is a must-read for studying history. The current popular edition is the Qianlong Wuying Palace edition of the Qing Dynasty. It is said that after the Commercial Press printed the Sibu Congkan in 1920, it had a proposal to reprint the ancient edition of the Twenty-Four Histories. After ten years of accumulation, it has finally gathered momentum, and sample prints have been released for sale and pre-ordering. Anyone who has seen the samples says that the synthesis of the whole book has several advantages: First, it is a great achievement to compile and combine old editions. Old editions from the Song and Yuan dynasties are rare and hard to find. In the past, public and private collectors could obtain several types of editions, which were already treasures. Now, the library has not only released all the collections of the Hanfen Tower, but also sought out more than ten types of Song and Yuan editions collected by collectors at home and abroad, which are extensive and rich, and can be called unprecedented. This example is also for the purpose of purchase and collection. Second, it is to correct the omissions of the Palace edition. The Wuying engraved edition is actually full of flaws, and there is no detailed explanation of it in the past. That is, the Ming Southern Supervision edition and the Jigu Pavilion edition, which are valued by the world, are not completely based on the original engraving of the Song and Yuan Dynasties. Now, according to the good edition obtained, all the missing texts, wrong characters, duplicate pages, blank spaces, etc. of the Palace edition can be corrected. This is convenient for collation. Third, the printing of the whole book is exquisite. The Commercial Press's printing technology is exquisite. The previous prints of the Hundred Naps Records of the Grand Historian and the Naps Edition of the Zizhi Tongjian, etc., are not inferior to the original engraving. The reproduced books can obtain the true face and are far better than the reproduced and engraved versions. As for the school according to, it is said that it is more prudent, and there is no need to sweep the leaves to prevent the disadvantages of arbitrarily changing it. This book is a treasure book that must be purchased by public and private libraries and book collectors, and it is especially suitable for those who already have the Palace edition of the Twenty-Four Histories to be equipped with it for review.

German Harmony School Opens Summer School 75

The German Harmony School on Bin Road in the Public Concession of the city was expanded into a two-level primary school this spring, accommodating nearly two hundred students, most of whom are poor children. Therefore, the school's finances are still not adequate. During the summer vacation, a Japanese language specialization department has been opened for secondary school students and above to specialize in Japanese language. The teachers have studied in Japan for more than ten years and have rich educational experience. It is planned to use the tuition fees collected to subsidize the German Harmony School. The number of applicants has been very enthusiastic in recent days, and it is also heard that a primary school tutoring class will be opened at the same time, divided into day and night classes.

A Word or Two • Dragon 79

The more intelligent a person is, the less opinion they have. Therefore, they have more unsatisfactory things than stupid people.

The struggle in the realm of love is like a warlord's chaos, there will always be a day of victory or bloodshed.

The many students are the future masters of the country, and their importance is no less than that of flowers and rice, which are related to the national economy and the people's livelihood, but the government's heart to cultivate students should be as deep as the farmer's heart to love and protect flowers and rice.

If you stain a little ink on your clothes, you will be eager to wash the bar. If you secretly do an evil thing, you will be happy and contented, so the human heart is unpredictable and the world is rugged.

If you don't know the price of rice, you don't know thrift. If you don't know the shame of national humiliation, you don't know self-strengthening. The effect of passive excitement is also conceivable.

When young people are studying, they all want to make a great career in the future. By the time they leave school, they are either warlords who lose power and humiliate the country, or officials who plunder the land, or treacherous merchants who act as accomplices for tigers, or thieves who transport rice for export. Half of them are indeed because of economic coercion, and half of them are still confused by the inducement of a bad environment.

The benevolent family only knows how to seek life, but does not know how to pay attention to hygiene, so every summer there are rescues that cannot be saved, and they are exhausted from running around.

If you entertain guests in the summer, it is well-intentioned, but it may turn into ill will, because they disturb you with a lot of Dongli things that are easy to get sick, so it is best to avoid banquets in the summer.

If a person wants to avoid the invasion of disease demons in the summer, he only needs not to be too cool when sleeping, avoid raw and cold food when eating, and refuse all kinds of banquets, and that's it.

On the Nanzhang, Jin and Xuan, the Origin of Revolutionary Strategies 80

Nanzhang is the hometown of Sun Yat-sen, the mentor of the Chinese Revolution, located forty li away from the county seat in the Fourth and Da Du [collectively known as the Four Da and Two Du]. It is also known as Nanzhang Market because there is a town called Nanzhang Market in that area, hence the name. When people ask about the hometown of the locals, they don't say a certain village in the Fourth or Da Du, but always answer Nanzhang, which is the custom. There are more than thirty villages with a population of about 40,000. The people are kind and good, and it is the first village in the county. Many people go out to make a living and are considered rich and prosperous. Since the revolution, there have been many people from this area who have worked for the party and the country. In addition to Sun Yat-sen and his son from Cuikeng, there is Mr. Lu Haodong, who died in Guangzhou and was from the same village as Sun Yat-sen, President Cheng Yutang from Anding, Minister Li Luchao from Qishan, and Commander Ouyang Ju from Mazi, all of whom have attracted national attention. The revolutionary figures in Nanzhang did not begin with Sun Yat-sen, but there were two people before him, one was Tan Shaoguang from Yakou and the other was Liang Zizhi from Longxuetou. Anyone who reads the history of the Taiping Rebellion knows Tan Shaoguang, but very few people in the county know about Liang Zizhi, and he is almost forgotten. Zizhi was a poor Confucian scholar who taught in the countryside to make a living. After the failure of the Taiping Rebellion, Zizhi was angry at the Manchus' wanton killing and saddened by the Han traitors' lack of patriotism. So he secretly gathered the villagers and wanted to attack Gong County. However, there was no opportunity. There was a tradition in the village that during the Dragon Boat Festival, there would be a parade in the city. The local custom was to welcome the gods and hold parades on the Dragon Boat Festival, either day or night, which was the most lively festival of the year. Zizhi then conspired with the villagers to hide weapons in giant bamboo, and entered the city one day in advance, pretending to be needed for holding fire, wanting to attack without warning. Unfortunately, the plan was revealed and Zizhi was martyred. Therefore, people in the city now have the saying [Old villagers dragging green bamboo] to ridicule the villagers, but they do not know that this saying is a memorial to the national spirit of the villagers. In the old days of autocracy, people mostly did not dare to talk about Zizhi's anecdotes. Although the two did not achieve great success, after more than two hundred years, the foreign emperors were finally overthrown by Sun Yat-sen. If they have knowledge in the afterlife, they should also be proud. Who knows but that the one who destroys Qin is not Chu? Nanzhang is truly worthy of being the source of revolutionary strategies. (Que Chou)

Textual Research on Xianshan · Yang · One · Xiao

The martyr Chen Yingshi was buried in Xianshan outside the South Gate of Huzhou. However, Xianshan is not only found in Huzhou. It has been researched that there is also Xianshan in Xiangyang Prefecture, Hubei. In the past, Yang You loved mountains and rivers. Every time there was a beautiful scenery, he would go to Xianshan to set up wine and talk forever. He sighed with emotion and said to Zou Zhan and others, "Since the universe existed, there has been this mountain. Since then, there have been many virtuous scholars who have climbed this mountain and looked into the distance, like me and you. They have all been submerged and unheard of, making people sad. If I have knowledge after a hundred years, my ghost will still climb this mountain." Zhan said, "Your fame and reputation will surely be passed on along with this mountain." After You died, the people of Xiangyang built a monument and temple on Xianshan. Those who looked at the monument could not help but shed tears. Du Yu named it the "Tear-Dropping Monument," which is also a famous place.

Mosihu Lake 81

Spring Tide

Mosihu Lake is located outside the Shuixi Gate of the capital, and it is said to be the best of the forty-eight scenic spots in Beijing. I recently visited and felt that although its scenery is simple and beautiful, it is not as broad and beautiful as Xuanwu Lake. When the setting sun is infinitely good in the evening, sitting here and having a clear conversation while holding tea is also a joy in life.

The temple in charge of this lake is called Huayan Temple, and its multi-storied pavilions and buildings are quite good. The center is the Yu Jintang and the top is the Shengqi Building. According to old history, Xu Da and the Ming Taizu once gambled here. Da won, and the Taizu gave him this lake. After Da's death, the lake's production still belonged to Xu's descendants for hundreds of years. Recently, it was heard that the Beijing Municipal Government has already requisitioned it for public ownership. The monks of Huayan Temple were all driven away, and more than 10,000 yuan was given to Xu's descendants as compensation and reorganized into Mosihu Lake Park. The Education Bureau and the Finance Bureau each sent a staff member to be stationed here to manage everything. Therefore, the lake has been quite bureaucratic recently.

From the side door of Yu Jintang, a winding path leads to the Zeng Gong Pavilion. The view of the lake here is the most refreshing, making people feel broad-minded. That day, I was with Qin Wang and other gentlemen, and we sat here to drink tea. At that time, the twilight was slightly shrouded, and the setting sun had disappeared behind the mountains. The scenery on the lake was all faded. The opposite Qingliang Mountain could still be seen clearly, and the city walls were like a belt, which was extremely beautiful. We talked and laughed, pointing and pointing, until all the other guests had left before we left. It was already seven o'clock when we looked at the watch.

I heard that the scenery of watching lotus flowers in Mochou Lake is the most beautiful. We went to visit, but it was not the right time, which made us feel quite regretful. At the same time, I felt that this is a waterside view, but one cannot boat. As Xuanwu Lake can be rowed in the middle of the stream, its ability to attract tourists is slightly inferior. However, the buildings on the lake have the flavor of West Lake villas, and there are many couplets, many of which are excellent. I only remembered that a certain gentleman's couplet said: People call Mochou Lake, call Mochou. There are originally many things to worry about in the world. Wang Ding has an image, and it should be like him. There are not many people in the eyes who are like this. I feel that it is quite clever and can be recited.

Adjacent to Mochou Lake is the Yue Army Cemetery, which was for those who sacrificed in the founding of the Republic of China. Mr. Zhongzhi personally wrote an inscription, "Establish the Country and Become Benevolent." There are two giant steles next to it, which seem to be tomb inscriptions written by Tan Zu'an and Wang Jingwei. The characters have been blurred and cannot be recognized. During the era of warlord autocracy, the local officials did not pay attention to this tomb, so the dilapidated walls and weeds were full of it. Since the revolutionary army recovered the capital, it has been slightly renovated, a new pavilion has been built, and a stone railing has been added in front of the stele road. However, as no one is in charge, it still feels desolate.

Based on my experience of traveling around the famous scenic spots in Beijing, the top of Qingliang Mountain is suitable for overlooking the entire view of Beijing, Linggu Temple is suitable for holding a picnic, Xuanwu Lake is suitable for boating on a moonlit night, and Mochou Lake is suitable for watching the rain in the autumn morning. I don't know if there are any tourists in Beijing who feel the same way as me.

Travel Notes in Nanyang (39) Linghua

However, the difficulty in resolving the male-female system is the same as the economic problem highly advocated by Marx. A Jin person once told me that there is a folk saying in my place that people in Jiangnan first engrave their original examination papers after passing the imperial examination, and people in Shanxi first marry a concubine after passing the imperial examination. From this, it can be seen that the customs in China, regardless of wealth or status, men never fail to indulge their sexual desires once they achieve success. At the same time, they still use the morality of "three obediences and four virtues" to restrain their wives and concubines. It is incomprehensible that all morality and shame are only set for women. However, the difficulty in resolving the sex problem is equal to the economic problem. The West does not use the concubine system, but replaces it with free divorce, and recently even replaces it with free love. In fact, the changes are even greater, but they are more equal than in the East. My Buddha then established a monastic system, which is too high and difficult to practice. Many practitioners fail, and Buddhism in China is in line with Confucianism's polygamy system. Buddhism in Qinghai and Tibet is also in line with the Tibetan custom of polyandry. Then, Buddhism in the West must also be in line with the free love of the lover system. Great is my Buddhist door, how can it be confined to one pattern? In the future, will the one who can liberate everything be the joyous Buddhist system of Mongolia?

However, I know that Mr. Xiong Changqing's family organization is not like the polygamy system of ordinary capitalists, who use women to provide for their entertainment. Mr. Xiong originally wanted to run a girls' school, but people added rumors to it. He then had a whimsical idea to widely recruit female guests to teach them. The system is that those who enter his Fuyuan, in addition to food and lodging, receive eight yuan per month for all expenses. It is stipulated that those who wish to leave can leave at any time. If they meet on the road in the future, they can only call Mr. Xiong. But those who have left do not have to come again. I once went to his Fuyuan and saw the situation of practicing arts in classes, and I knew that Xiong was a strange person who was curious and used the method of Lord Mengchang to support guests to adopt many poor girls and teach them technology. His female guests rarely decorate themselves and are all simple and accustomed to things. Mr. Xiong is probably a female Mengchang who is hospitable. Now, the male Mengchang raises thousands of warriors who go out and kill people, and no one dares to criticize it. The female Mengchang raises female guests to practice arts, but people criticize it. Is it not unfair? Xiong sent me two lines of poetry, saying, "Please see the Jingwei River in Fuyuan, which does not invade each other." This can reveal his ambition.

On the eighth day, I discussed poetry with the poets of the Tanxie Poetry Society, and there were also monks who were able to write poetry. The literary style overseas is also quite elegant. The most prominent literary celebrity here is Qiu Shuyuan, who has written many works. He is a chivalrous and hospitable person. During the Wuxu Reform, he entertained the new party and spent a lot of money. He is still a literary star overseas. It is a pity that he is old and sick and cannot go out. Qiu's selection of the manuscripts of the Tanxie Poetry Society shows that Qiu has studied both the Han and Song schools and admires Yuan Zicai very much when discussing poetry. His daughter, named Mingquan, is famous for her art. Her husband, Wang Laisu, graduated from Peking University. I hope he can promote Mr. Qiu's literary style. Qiu also understands Buddhism and once edited the Lion's Roar newspaper. It is a pity that Qiu is sick and there is no successor. The Buddhist light of Nanyang culture has greatly faded.

Trivial Talk on Waxberries 82

Xiao Chang

As the saying goes, "The waxberries are red all over the mountains at the summer solstice." It is now the time of the summer solstice, so waxberries are on the market again.

The most famous area for waxberries in Zhejiang is Tanglou in western Zhejiang and Zhuji in eastern Zhejiang. Other places such as Yuyao and Xiaoshan also produce this fruit, but the production is far less than that of Tanglou and Zhuji, and the quality is not as good.

The quality of waxberries in Tanglou and Zhuji is different, and the taste is also different. The waxberries produced in Tangqi are mostly charcoal waxberries, which are large in size, thick in grain, small in pit, and have a lot of juice. The taste is extremely sweet and is indeed a good product. The waxberries produced in Zhuji are small in size, have small stems, fine grains, thick pits, and less juice, but the taste is fresh, which is not as good as the waxberries produced in Tangqi. However, the ripening period is later and can only be harvested after the Tangqi products have been on the market. When the waxberries are ripe on the branches, they are very beautiful to look at. The green leaves and red fruits look like colorful sedan chairs.

When the waxberries in Tangqi are ripe on the branches, pedestrians can eat them at will. The owner of the food sees it and does not prohibit it, but when eating, they must not pick them off with their hands. They must eat them directly from the branches with their mouths. If they are picked off with their hands, they will be regarded as stealing. The surface of the waxberries has awns, and after picking them, they must be lightly rubbed with the palm to remove the awns before they can be eaten in large quantities, otherwise, if you eat several of them, the palate and tongue in the mouth will be injured by the awns.

Waxberry pits have the effect of eliminating hair in our stomachs, so those who eat waxberries must swallow several pits every year. And the people in the southern countryside of Wukang swallow all the pits they eat, no matter how many they eat. This is another anecdote about eating waxberries.

The publishing industry news is always known for its vividness, and the Saturday newspaper is becoming more and more exciting. It has now been published to issue 363. The second collection has been released for sale, and the binding and paper are very exquisite. The printing is especially fresh and original. There are a total of more than 340 sensual copperplate illustrations. It is said to sell for only one yuan and two jiao.

Chapter 12: Farewell Banquet and Departure, Plucking Flowers to Keep a Beautiful Shadow, Grand Gathering in a Famous Garden, Tea Tasting to See the Beautiful Appearance

Ruiyun had a face like the red glow of the setting sun, and a pair of eyes sparkling like the stars in the sky. It was a pity that although she had the freshness of the rising sun, she was numbed because her profession was a prostitute. Even if the seeds of love occasionally sprouted in her emotional field, they could not grow out. As the ancients said, [It is not that there are no sprouts, but the cattle and sheep graze on them.] Therefore, her concept was to listen to people's arrangements and be content with the situation. Moreover, she was a sacrifice that was bought. She was a person who was called a "pleaser" in the brothel and had no power to resist. She was almost not allowed to complain, just like a news reporter under strict censorship. Although she was full of complaints, she could not publish a sentence. Therefore, her body and spirit had to be controlled by others. That night, one stick of incense and one meal of big dishes lasted until half past eleven. The three mouths of the three people were really too busy. Today, it was like working overtime, eating and chatting. Ruiyun originally wanted to ask Zuo Shichen to go take pictures together tomorrow afternoon. Zuo Shichen said, "You go with A Jin. However, A Jin said that the meaning of the old madam was that Ruiyun's business would definitely decline after she got married. Could you please help the second young master? The current Han Yun is not very good. She can't even sing in the front row. It would be good if she could sing in the second row. Zuo Shichen agreed casually. She wanted to pass on this business forever. Suddenly, a festival passed, and suddenly seven or eight days passed. At that time, many people in the brothel officially announced that they were getting married. What was previously hidden can now be officially announced. Many suspected rumors that someone was getting married have now been confirmed. People who were creating an atmosphere are still running their business, and the rumors are not denied but are self-evident. To prove that she is married, you only need to go to the newspaper with a urging flower charm and say that so-and-so's sign is gone, or the sign is still there, but the person who is called has changed into a beautiful posture. Although it is not that the phoenix has left and the building is empty, things are no longer the same. So, it is as if a new dynasty has been replaced, and a new group of people has taken the stage to replace the group of people who have married. Among these new people, there must be a group of outstanding people, beautiful women, who are called the rising stars. From ancient times to the present, which society is not like this? From the vast sky to the small flower or leaf, why is the brothel society alone different?

The Financial Gold Market is Getting Worse 83

The total drop in the last three days was thirty-seven taels

The floating gains outside of six hundred taels were greatly affected

The long foreign exchange was loose and the gold price plummeted. Yesterday's gold auction had an alarming change. The rampant decline was indescribable. The turmoil was fierce, but there were always four or five taels of hidden risks. People were extremely fearful and suddenly plummeted by more than twenty taels. This was really affected by the easing of foreign exchange. Although the banks were taking in, they were not diligent. In particular, the major firms such as Yuan Xingyong, Yuansheng, Jin Dayong, etc. were very eager to sell. Those with floating gains outside of six hundred taels were greatly affected. Moreover, the bank closure was approaching, and each firm was eager to sell, so the market atmosphere suddenly became weak and suddenly broke through the 580 tael mark. The high and low prices in half a day actually differed by more than twenty-eight taels, which was rare. Although the major firms were long in the morning, buyers were active in the market. Fuchang, Yuan Maoyong, Zhifengyong, etc. all had purchases, so the opening price returned high. Then it jumped to more than 604 taels, but the flowers flashed and went in the opposite direction. Foreign exchange also listed a long order. Major firms eagerly sold off and plummeted. The decline was rapid and fell tragically by more than twenty taels, suddenly within 580 taels. Until noon, it suddenly turned flat and jumped up seven or eight taels, and then the buyers slightly saw a stop. Finally, it stood between 584 taels. However, the industry was still in a fog. How could there be such a big change in the evening?

The first order revealed a high opening and a flash. Yesterday, the Bank of England released a long of sixteen and seven points. The US silver added one-half. The exchange rate did not move. The opening price of gold in August immediately added three taels and one qian. Then it continued to increase by four or five taels. The foreign exchange was still flat. Guangbang and others settled for six pence and two five for September British gold. The China Banking Corporation mutually did US$36.9375, so when the first order was revealed, it rose to 604 taels and five qian. However, the listing price had already added two five US$0.375. The Japanese gold decreased by two points and each firm sold it vigorously. In addition, the internal transfer of the draft was declining, so the situation got worse and worse, and the price plummeted by more than twenty taels. At half past ten, it was 84 taels and a half. Afterwards, it was raised again by more than four taels, but it was bought by four or five taels of Qipu Zhuyou and Shanghai. The September British gold was six pence and six two five, and the October one was seven five.

Drafts were loose and broke through the 80 tael mark. After 11 o'clock, the decline was even more severe. Xiangyu, Yuan Xingyong, and each firm bravely sold off. The recent bank buying price of Japanese gold was only one tael, three qian, one fen. The September British gold was difficult to sell even at six pence and six eight seven five, so the gold price continued to fall crazily by twelve or thirteen taels and suddenly broke through the 80 tael mark. At half past eleven, it suddenly entered 76 taels. Afterwards, there was a slight replenishment of the head position on the table. Special Issue for the 5th Anniversary of Shanghai Minzhi Elementary and Middle School 87

Inscription by Zhu Yingpeng

The Past and Future of Our School by Xu Renhan and Gong Bing

Our school, in the spring of the 14th year of the Republic of China, leased five buildings in Runde Lane, Moore Road, Shanghai Public Concession, and set up a preparatory office at No. 18, Taixing Lane, nearby. In the summer of the same year, we moved into the school building and named it Minzhi Public School, opening a summer school with six teachers and three students, teaching diligently. In the autumn semester, school board members Ma Chonggan, Cai Xingsu, female poet Chen Jiaqing, Fudan University Bachelor of Science Zhang Tianjun, Jiangsu Provincial Second Normal School graduate Ding Zhuangru, Xu Xiongwan, Second Women's Normal School graduate Bao Huishu, Yanshi Girls' School graduate Sun Jie, and other teachers were hired to teach in elementary and middle schools. In that year, the number of elementary, middle, and kindergarten students increased from 33 to 75. In the spring of the 15th year, a library was added. In January of the 16th year, a publishing department was established to publish Chinese language achievements and the first issue of the school journal. In the autumn of the 17th year, due to the increase of students to 328, the school building was insufficient, so we moved to Weifeng Lane, Weihaiwei Road. In September of the same year, due to the accumulation of winning manuscripts from previous Shanghai speech competitions, we published a collection of speeches for our comrades. On January 17th of the 18th year, we were approved and registered by the Shanghai Special City Education Bureau. In the summer of the same year, we were ordered to change our name to Minzhi Elementary and Middle School. In the autumn of the same year, the number of students increased to 412, and the school building was again insufficient, so we leased a Western-style building at No. 121 on the same road to create a second campus. In the spring of the 19th year, the Western-style building at No. 105 adjacent to the second campus happened to be available for rent, which could accommodate four or five hundred people, so we gave up the Weifeng Lane building and rented this one instead. By this point, the school building was slightly more spacious and suitable, and both teachers and students felt more convenient for teaching and learning. This year, we added a women's department, an adult class, a people's school, and a sports field. The number of faculty and staff increased to 26, and the student body increased to 558. The organization was divided into two kindergarten levels, twelve elementary school levels for boys and girls, two junior high school levels, one adult level, and two people's school levels, for a total of 19 classes, forming a rough scale. For the past five years, we have worked tirelessly throughout the year, actively engaging in publishing, speeches, libraries, physical education, hygiene, and other activities that are beneficial to the physical and mental well-being of children and youth, striving to achieve the goal of establishing a successful Chinese-run education in the concession. This is a brief history of our school's past five years, which can be reported to our fellow countrymen and gentlemen. However, as the number of students increases daily, according to our school's three-year plan, we plan to increase the kindergarten to four levels, the elementary school to 24 levels for boys and girls in the spring and autumn semesters, the middle school to six levels, the adult supplementary class to two levels, the people's school to six levels, and to add two levels of commercial supplementary classes, for a total of 44 levels. Based on the past increase in the proportion of students and the current surge in the population of the western district, it is indeed possible to achieve this. However, since our school does not have its own school building, it is feared that it will be difficult to improve internally and develop each year for a long time to come. The colleagues have been thinking about the many students who have been together day and night for five years, and there is no shortage of talented and hardworking people. If there is no well-equipped school building to make great achievements and attract more students, it is not a great plan to reserve talents for the country and recover the right to education. However, purchasing land and constructing buildings requires a huge amount of money, and the wish is grand but the strength is weak, so we are hesitant. We hope that our school's alumni, students' families, and enthusiastic educators at home and abroad will provide support so that we can see success as soon as possible. Now that our school is compiling and printing a special issue for the fifth anniversary, we respectfully present the school history to our fellow countrymen.

Eulogy (Wang Boqun)

There is no greater joy in the world than holding the power of education, especially when a school is created from scratch, from elementary school to middle school, from dozens of students to hundreds, and from hundreds to almost a thousand. They come with books and leave after graduation, going on to further education or serving society. Like planting a forest, I see it becoming a shade; like planting good grain, I see it yielding a rich harvest. What joy is there! However, the care, cultivation, and protection from the wind, rain, cold, and heat have also been laborious. As the saying goes, "First hardship, then gain." Benevolent people use this to cultivate new knowledge.

I know Mr. Xu Renhan, the founder of Shanghai Minzhi Middle School, and I rejoice in his tireless efforts and remarkable achievements. Signed Wang Chonghui.

Preface (Wei Ke)

Minzhi Middle School is about to compile and print a fifth anniversary album and asked me to write a preface. I believe that [Minzhi] is one of the few private schools in western Shanghai with remarkable achievements and has long been trusted by the people of western Shanghai. Looking back at the establishment of [Minzhi], it has only been five years, but its rapid development can be described as a thousand miles a day. The future progress is immeasurable.

Although schools are divided into public and private in terms of finance and management, the purpose of education is the same. There are many school-age children in the Shanghai Concession, but the schools run by the工部局 are few, and there are not many municipal schools either. The only reliance for meeting the educational needs of the concession is private schools. Therefore, private schools bear the most important educational responsibility in the Shanghai Concession.

Education is the foundation of a country. Now that our country is building a nation based on the Three Principles of the People, the purpose of education should naturally be based on the Three Principles of the People. At the moment, the call for the recovery of educational buildings in the concession is rising. The reason for this is to achieve the education of the Three Principles of the People. [Minzhi] has not been established for long, but its achievements are remarkable. The future efforts and development are immeasurable. I hope that the officials in charge of school affairs will pay special attention to the realization of the Three Principles of the People's education, so that the equipment, curriculum, teaching methods, extracurricular activities, and other facilities are in line with the original purpose of the Three Principles of the People's education, and become a model for concession education. Then, it will not only be the fortune of [Minzhi] but also the fortune of education.

The standard of society

The closing speech for the fifth anniversary of our school (Dai Langhua)

China cannot even talk about education now because most people simply do not understand the necessity of seeking knowledge. The gap between the propertied class and the proletariat is too great. Most rich people rely on their inheritance and power to live without having to seek a living, believing that studying is a painful thing. They do not know that not allowing their children to study is like not allowing them to take the road to self-renewal. As for poor families, they cannot even take care of their basic needs of food, clothing, and shelter, so where would they get the money to provide for education? Therefore, the results on both sides are equivalent to a lack of knowledge. Since the people's knowledge is not widespread, how can the country be strong? Therefore, the strength of the country depends entirely on the development of the people's knowledge.

Therefore, we should first thank the two principals of our school and congratulate them on their success. Our school has been established for five years and has overcome many difficulties to achieve five years of honor and social trust. We should thank them for laying a solid foundation for the future generations of the country to resist the oppression of the great powers and promote people's intelligence so that China can turn from weak to strong. There is another spirit that is even more admirable, that is, the two principals do not hesitate to sacrifice their spirit and money to seek happiness for the society and the country and be pioneers in the education field. Past achievements have been established, and we should work harder to seek future hope. The spirit of cooperation between teachers and students, on the one hand, teachers are enthusiastic about teaching, and students should keep the future of the country in mind. Students, on the other hand, must cultivate excellent knowledge, noble personality, and strong physique in the school to prepare for the future masters and achieve the final goal. This is my hope for the fifth anniversary of our school.

What We Want to Say About the Fifth Anniversary of Our School (Jiang Nianqu)

Photograph of the tenth session of female students from the elementary, middle, and kindergarten (Photograph by Wang Kai)

In China, which is oppressed by imperialism, there are many people who have not received education due to economic difficulties. However, it is not without a remedy. Although our country has a considerable plan for educational facilities, there is a great lack of talent to guide reading. Therefore, education cannot keep pace with the countries of the world. The two founders of this school are very enthusiastic about education. They want to save our country and solve the suffering of people who do not know how to read, so they founded this school, named Minzhi, which means to enlighten the people's intelligence.

In the midst of difficulties and hardships, five years have passed unconsciously. In these five weeks, the enthusiastic efforts of the founders and teachers have achieved very good results. It is so difficult to run a school in this concession, but the two founders followed the fearless spirit of the President and unyieldingly created a good foundation for Chinese-run schools in the concession. Such talents are truly worthy of my admiration. Furthermore, in the past five years, the atmosphere of this school has been very good. The students in the school have a competitive mentality towards their studies, and the students are very enthusiastic about patriotic movements. Another characteristic that is different from other schools is that the clothes worn by the students are very clean and simple, without any thought of showing off, and are completely civilianized. This state should be preserved by future students, and do not let the students in the school become aristocratic after another fifth anniversary. Now there is a difficulty in this school, and this school should solve it quickly in the shortest possible time, which is the problem of the school building. It is hoped that a large school building will be built, so that the school will develop day by day and the number of students will increase day by day, and the school building will not be crowded, and it will be good to build its own school building without having to pay huge rents and transfer this money to construction. It is also more reassuring for students to study. However, where does this huge amount of money come from? We must ask the enthusiastic people in the country to make some efforts to promote the school's advocacy of enlightening the people's intelligence. These are the words I want to say.

The Spirit That This School Should Have in the Future by Hong Fanjun

There are many schools in Shanghai, but the quality is not consistent. There is no way to distinguish between them, and they often tend to go to church schools. Chinese school operators do not take reserving talents for the country as their policy, but transfer to personal interests. Therefore, the obstruction of education is as before. Now the principal of this school is aware of this and runs the school wholeheartedly and sincerely. Based on years of experience, the principal of this school has been planning to establish a small-scale school in the spring of the 14th year. At the beginning of the school, everything was unable to compete with other schools, because the face was not enough. However, thanks to the principal's continuous efforts and the enthusiastic teaching of the professors, more and more scholars came and the reputation gradually increased. The school building became wider and wider, and the equipment inside gradually became more perfect. Outside, the speeches often won awards. The achievements of the five years were quite remarkable, but how could the five years of a hundred years of education limit the unlimited education career? Although the development of the future can be based on the achievements of the five years, it also lies in the principal's continued efforts. Since this school has had past achievements, it is not difficult to reach the peak and make foreign schools unable to prevail, so that students know where to go. As a pioneer in recovering the educational rights of the concession, the spirit that should be possessed in this anniversary is enough.

Bond Prices Plummet After Settlement 88

Yesterday, the bond market futures were lively, especially in the afternoon. Apart from the sluggish "Financial No Market," "96," "Continued Roll," and "Seven-Year Continued 25," the "Demobilization," "Customs Tariff Reduction of Troops," and others saw significant price fluctuations and brisk trading. "Whole Six Good Omen" was also active. However, the spot market remained very quiet. The bond market sentiment was poor, and confidence was weak, with supply exceeding demand. Therefore, it was weak from the initial opening in the morning, and the decline intensified later. Demobilization futures almost collapsed and stopped trading. Although they rebounded slightly in the afternoon, they still fell by a substantial three yuan. Customs Tariff and Demobilization fell by about two yuan, and Whole Six Good Omen also fell by one yuan and several jiao. The spot trading volume was 26,000 yuan, and futures exceeded 10 million yuan.

Cotton Yarn: Sharp Decline in the Yarn Market

The yarn market's downward trend has resurfaced, with rapid changes in recent days. The fundamental reason is the decline in the global cotton market, reduced consumption in various countries, and overproduction, making it difficult to be optimistic. It is said that there is a stockpile of over 300,000 bales of Japanese yarn, which is difficult to resolve immediately. Therefore, the previous day's sharp decline was followed by a slight rebound of 20 yuan, but today it fell again by 5 yuan. American cotton is also hovering around 13.25 cents due to lack of demand and abundant inventory, with good weather for new cotton. The local sales of yarn are quite scarce, as exorbitant rice prices and turbulent situations have greatly weakened the purchasing power of various groups. The bottom goods everywhere were mentioned yesterday.

Deteriorating Human Bids Remain Weak: The opening of the human bid market was met with a drop in the price of American cotton, causing a sudden drop in confidence. With few buyers, the selling pressure was particularly strong, with each bid falling by 6-7 qian. News of sluggish sales in the second and third rounds and a large drop in raw cotton prices further weakened the situation, with each bid falling by 6 qian to 1 liang 1 qian to 1 liang 3 qian. The afternoon opening was very weak, with widespread panic, and each bid fell by 5-6 qian. In the second round, the Hengda factory purchased 200 pieces per bid for the July and August contracts, giving the market a boost. The third round rose by 2-3 qian, and the closing price rose again by 2-3 qian, resulting in good prices. 123 qian were sold, with Jifeng, Hengyi, Daji, Yuantai, Tianlong, Shenchang, and Yiyu selling 500 to 2,600 bales, and Hengda, Tongyu, Hanfeng, Shenji, Dafeng, and Xincheng buying 500 to 1,050 bales. The total transaction volume was 25,150 bales. The closing prices of the human bids are recorded below:

Among them, 925 bales were purchased by fellow traders. The price dropped by 2.5 qian to 7.5 qian. Among the purchasing groups, the Guangdong group purchased the most, totaling 235 bales. In addition, 280 bales were purchased by inland groups, 175 bales by Tianjin groups, 80 bales by Hankou groups, 115 bales by Shantou groups, 280 bales by Niuzhuang groups, 40 bales by Changsha groups, and 75 bales by miscellaneous groups.

The Underlying Condition of the Cotton Market Amid the Sharp Decline 89

The drastic decline in the cotton market is mainly due to the global cotton market's downturn. Additionally, the trend of gold prices falling and the exchange rate loosening has made Indian cotton prices relatively cheaper. Many retail investors holding long positions, seeing the unfavorable environment, have had to painfully liquidate their positions. Furthermore, Ruida Company alone sold more than 10,000 dan, causing the market price to decline further, resembling a river flowing downwards. The attitude of various factories is unusually calm, and the situation in the cotton market is very weak. The Han Biao market is full of selling pressure. At the opening of the Han Biao market, the prices of American cotton and yarn fell, causing a sharp drop in confidence. Moreover, large investors were selling off, with each falling by 4 qian, 6.5 qian to 7 qian. In the afternoon, prices fell another 1-2 qian. Hengyi, Gongtai, Daji, Ruida, Yicheng, Yuantai, Changfeng, Shenxin, Tianlong, Hengde, and Yichang sold 1,000 to 11,000 dan, while Shenyu, Rongxing, Taixing, Yongfeng, Tongxing, Shenda, Tianchang, and Xincheng bought 1,100 dan to 3,000 dan. The fluctuations of Three-Grade Yarn and the changes in the Eastern Exchange Rate have progressed in inverse proportion. Recently, the Japanese market has plummeted again, seeing a low price of 98 yuan, with only a difference of over 10 yuan from the new low price of Min San. The arrival of Japanese yarn in Shanghai is already a favorable and formidable threat, and its impact is immediately visible. American Cooperative Absorbs Raw Cotton 93

Better Progress in Cotton Assessment: Cotton Demand Still Stagnant

A telegram on the 27th reported on the cotton market situation for the week, stating that the cotton price decline began in mid-July. The reasons for this decline were the settlement of the July contract and news of warmer weather and faster development of Southern cotton crops. However, when the new transaction market price for the October contract reached 12.5 cents, the decline stopped due to increased demand from traders and short covering. The number of unsettled long positions for the July contract was significantly higher than expected by various parties. On Wednesday of the week, the cooperative quickly absorbed the announced sale of 114,000 bales. On Thursday, it absorbed some more. At the end of the week, the July contract market was firmer than before. The Central cotton belt currently needs rain, and the recent high temperatures in the South have caused some unease. In other respects, the progress of the new cotton crop is better than before. Merchants expect the private report on the cotton production situation at the end of the month to have a higher figure compared to previous reports.

Furthermore, people in the cotton market believe that the market price has reached a level where it is possible to buy, and the stock market has better sentiment, so the buying trend has slightly increased. The high temperature in the central part of the cotton industry has caused some concern, but it is not yet considered a major event. Cotton crops are progressing well, spot demand is sluggish, and cotton trade remains quiet. The weekend statistics are attached below (unit: thousands of bales):

Grain: Lower River Rice Market Opens Within Limits

Yesterday, the source of goods at Zhabei was still scarce, and most of the registered cargo customers had already sold within the limit. This matter was resolved after the Social Bureau declared that it would be handled by the Bureau and then assigned to the rice shops. The commission for all rice merchants will be temporarily registered, and after the inventory is cleared, it will be jointly distributed. Therefore, most of the cargo customers, seeing the environment like this and the weather getting hotter, and the cargo being delayed in the river for a long time, which is not appropriate, and only incurring losses if delayed, automatically sold to the authorities. The highest price for Northern Japonica rice was 21 yuan, and the second-best was slightly lower. Thin rice also followed the Japonica market. The total number of bushels throughout the day was estimated to be over 2,000 shi. The remaining inventory today and tomorrow may be cleared. Because Metamorphosis Yuan is in the fancy category, it will still be handled according to the previous regulations and sold through the rice merchant's sample platform. The large market saw weakness, with the high price for high-quality goods on the market being around 19.5 yuan.

Only one ship arrived at the Lower River in South Shanghai from the Tongli gang, and it was sold out on the same day. Metamorphosis Yuan, foreign sharp corners returned to small triangles. There was no Northern Japonica rice or early and late rice available on the market. The situation was extremely quiet.

Continued Weakness in Newly Arrived Foreign Rice 94

Yesterday, because a large batch of new foreign rice arrived, the importing merchants waited and watched. Therefore, the market opened with a soft trend, followed by more floating lots and the market becoming even softer. However, because Dumi limited its price, the source became even more balanced, and it will be even more difficult to arrive in the future. Because the inland market price is higher than the Shanghai market, vendors do not dare to try. Therefore, foreign rice is welcomed in this street. Although the passenger transportation has stopped, the market will turn stable again. As a result, it continued to be slightly lower by about 1 jiao compared to the previous market. The total market transaction was 7,000 bags of small grain at a price of 17 yuan 2.5 jiao, 3,000 bags of large grain at a price of 16 yuan 9 jiao, 1,000 bags of No. 1 Saigon at a price of 18 yuan 6.7 jiao, 1,500 bags of No. 2 at a price of 18 yuan 2.5 jiao, 500 bags of Min Dang at a price of 16 yuan 7.5 jiao, and 200 bags of Kagai at a price of 17 yuan 7.4 cents. In addition, there were also over 3,000 bags of various types of brown rice and road goods, with prices close to the small grain.

Total Number of Foreign Rice Arrivals and Sales This Year 95

This year, 5 million bags of foreign rice have arrived, with large and small grains exported from Leigon accounting for the majority. Saigon rice only accounts for one-third. About 1 million bags have not yet been loaded, and there are about hundreds of thousands of bags of road goods. There have been very few new transactions, with only less than 1,000 tons reported.

The Flour Market Presents a Withered State Again 96

Thick Factory Inventory... Sluggish Sales... Sharp Fall in the Gold Market

Yesterday, the flour market presented a withered state again. This month, because the delivery is near, being the last day of trading, the Northern gangs ultimately found the market value too high to be in line with their plans, and they rarely showed interest. Most investors with long positions, seeing that the factory's inventory is gradually becoming abundant and actual sales are sluggish, had to settle the futures for this month. Therefore, the opening price fell, and the lowest price returned to 2 liang 5 qian. The distant months were quite lively at the initial opening in the morning, but as the factories successively released their positions and the sharp fall in the gold market was heard, caution turned to softness, and it became sluggish. The situation was not good in the afternoon. Judging from the current market trend, factories and traders in the local market are not optimistic. Only the attitudes of the gangs in Wuxi, Suzhou, and other inland areas have remained unchanged, and they have frequently absorbed. Therefore, the high and low prices will only be determined when the news of Xiangfen's sales comes out. As a result, this month fell by 2 fen 7.5 li, July-August fell by a small 7.5 li, September fell by a small 1 fen 2.5 li, October fell by a small 2 fen 2.5 li, and November fell by a small 2 fen 2.5 li.

The Wheat Futures Market Finally Falls 97

Yesterday, the wheat futures market showed an initial firmness followed by a continued weakness in each month. In the morning, because the quoted price of foreign wheat was slightly better by 2-3 qian, people were thinking of rallying. However, in the afternoon, because the flour market turned weak and the gold price fell sharply again, the overall sentiment was inevitably affected. Observing the current market trend, the local factories and traders are not optimistic. Only the attitudes of the inland gangs in Wuxi and Suzhou have remained unchanged, and they have frequently absorbed. Therefore, the high and low prices will only be determined by the news of incense and flour sales. As a result, July-September fell by a small 3 fen each, August-November fell by a small 1 fen, and October fell by 2 fen. Because the arrival of spot wheat is smooth and the factory stomachs are average, each position is shouting for a lower price of around 3 fen. A total of 10,000 bags of wheat from Taizhou, Shashi, Nanjing, Gaoyou, Yangzhou, etc., and 800 bags of wheat from Zhenche were handled by Fuxin and Fufeng.

Acknowledgement

On the occasion of our school's fifth anniversary, we were honored to receive inscriptions from eminent scholars at home and abroad. The staff is deeply grateful and expresses their gratitude with a few words.

Respectfully, the staff of Minzhi Elementary and Middle School

Foreword 98

(Editor)

Time flies like an arrow. It has been five years since the establishment of our school. The staff is limited in knowledge and experience. We have worked hard for five years, and there have been times when we were in danger of failure. We believe that schools are public instruments of society, and the people of the country should first recognize them and then pay attention to them. In particular, the citizens of this city should use the space of Shenbao to briefly publish the school's management process and recent situation in words and photos, so that they can meet the people of the country and leave a considerable impression. This is the first reason why the staff has edited and printed this publication.

The school has only been managed for five years, and its history is still shallow, and its facilities are incomplete. Like a person, it is still in its infancy, its physical strength is insufficient, and its knowledge is immature. We hope that those who sympathize with the school will provide support and care, and that the intellectual community will provide guidance and correction, so that the school can progress with the years and last for a long time. This is the second reason why the staff has edited and printed this publication.

It is not that this is the only reason. The birth of our school originally had the mission of opening up people's minds and recovering educational rights. However, due to limited ability and insufficient strength, we have not yet completed it after five years of struggle. We believe that in the future, we should maintain the spirit of the past, gather the strength of the majority of comrades, divide the work and cooperate, and hold on with determination. Over time, we will definitely make the Chinese in the concession literate more and gradually recover educational rights invisibly, so that it will be of some help to national sovereignty, people's education, and social construction. On the occasion of the fifth anniversary, we will arouse the past and awaken the future, set a benchmark, and work together to achieve it, regardless of success or failure. This is the third reason why the staff has edited and printed this publication.

There is one more thing to mention. This publication is limited in scope and time, and there are inevitable omissions. We hope that all readers will provide more guidance to correct the shortcomings of the staff. We are currently working on editing and printing a commemorative album, which will be published after the weather cools down in autumn. At that time, we will seek corrections from all gentlemen again.

Theater News 100

The Star Film Company announces that "Romantic Woman" is a new romantic police film recently produced simultaneously with "Peach Blossom Lake" and "Water Margin" by this company. Since the start of filming, they have been working day and night. The leading role of "Romantic Woman" has been changed several times, and it was finally decided that the famous actress Xuan Jinglin would play the role. Since Xuan stopped acting, audiences of domestic films have missed her very much. This time, she returns to the screen and gets a role that fits her personality, which allows her to show her strengths. Since the news came out, letters inquiring about the release date have been pouring in every day. Director Cheng Bugao is dedicating himself fully to this film, and every scene is depicted with the latest directing techniques. The film will be completed in one or two weeks, and the release date is not far away.

The Zhongshan Grand Theater announces that it will be showing "Echo in the Empty Valley" directed by Ma-Xu Weibang starting today. This film has been shown in various theaters, and the box office and public opinion have been very good. This time, a French song and dance troupe that recently arrived in Shanghai has been hired to perform on stage, including Gypsy dance, Hawaiian dance, Yin Island dance, and Western closet scenes.

Qingfeng Garden

Service of This Year's Graduates from Jiaotong University

Before each year's graduates from Jiaotong University graduate, they are recruited with heavy money. This year's graduates are no exception. The Construction Committee has sent a letter requesting the employment of as many as fifteen students from the Electrical Engineering Department's Telecommunications program to serve as engineers in various electrical engineering projects. Students from the Power Engineering program have also received letters from many power plants both inside and outside the city requesting their employment. Many mechanical engineering students have also accepted employment from a large factory in this city. Those who have not been hired will be uniformly dispatched by the Ministry of Railways to various railway bureaus for service. Students from the Management School, because their studies are in specialized railway management, are uniformly dispatched by the Ministry of Railways to various routes for one year of internship, after which they will all be promoted to formal railway staff. This year's total of more than one hundred and twenty graduates, more than fifty people have been employed by outside parties, while those employed by the Ministry of Railways are only more than seventy people. Nowadays, in China, there is a surplus of people for positions, and it is very difficult for university graduates to seek employment. Therefore, the number of unemployed university graduates is countless. However, the Jiaotong University authorities are able to plan the students' future, so that graduates have no fear of unemployment and no need to change careers, in order to fulfill the Ministry of Railways' and the government authorities' original intention of cultivating specialized talents. Among all national universities, at most, they can only be responsible for introducing a few students with excellent grades, and it is impossible to introduce all of them. This move by the school is really commendable, and it is also due to its excellent results. (Duan)

Jiaotong University Hires a Sports Coach

Since Yuan Dongjun, a Far Eastern athlete, published his opinion that the reason for our country's failure in the Far Eastern Games was the lack of sports guidance, the Jiaotong University authorities have been able to accommodate Yuan's opinion and actively promote sports to strengthen students' bodies and promote our country's international spirit. Starting next semester, they have specially hired sports expert Shen Guoquan as the school's sports coach. Shen is Korean and graduated from Nanyang University in 1924. During his time at school, his athletic reputation had already spread far and wide. In the past, Nanyang's victory over the John Football Team was entirely due to Shen's efforts. After graduating, because his sports knowledge was not sufficient, he specially studied sports at the Teachers College of Columbia University in the United States for five years. In the United States, he participated in various competitions, and Americans were amazed by him. After returning to China last year, President Li of Jiaotong University wanted to hire him as the director of sports, but it did not happen for some reason. It has been decided to hire him as a sports coach and director next semester. The former director of the library, Huang Wenjian, resigned and went elsewhere, and the current director of sports, Tang Shuping, was transferred to fill the position of director of the library. The position of director of sports left by Tang will be filled by Shen. It is heard that in addition to Shen, Jiaotong University will also hire many sports coaches, all of whom are experts of the time. (Duan)

Our Principal

The newspapers these past few days have been busy publishing the graduation ceremonies of various schools. Our school has never published any literary works or discussions on educational issues, not to mention graduation ceremonies. Everything is in a state of silence, and there is no expectation of development. Although there are quite a few students in the school who study hard, most of them hold vague ideas. Their purpose in studying is because they have nothing to do, and studying is a pastime (I am also a student and do not intend to slander them). To know the current situation in China, graduates of Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School, Yin Weihua (photo by Chang Lie)

we students who have the opportunity to study should quickly work hard and move forward to create for society and find a way out for the nation. Where is the bright path? Our principal, although she has a kind of gentle smile, has not done anything to increase the students' knowledge and health. In terms of sports, she collected the students' sports fees, but there are no sports facilities, and there is no formal library, only a few mediocre English books and a few translated Chinese novels. I can't find a single magazine that is beneficial to the students. This is supposed to be reference material for us. Speaking of the teachers who are hired, except for one or two who understand teaching methods, the rest are here to solve their livelihood problems. I have already taken the wrong path into this kind of school.

The school's aim is that Chinese and English are equally important, so the graduation ceremony should of course be the same. But it is not like this. The English class graduates are all spirited and lively, sitting on the stage one by one to receive their diplomas. We Chinese graduates are all standing outside the door. I am not here for the sake of getting a diploma. In fact, what is the use of us getting a diploma that is almost equivalent to waste paper? However, although the principal is a Christian, she is not a foreigner.

A word to students who are transferring schools: when entering a school, be sure to carefully consider the content of the school. We want to gain practical knowledge, not study appearances. (Zhu Yun)

(1) The last page of the Sino-British Agreement on the Transfer of Weihaiwei, signed by Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting and British Minister to China Lampson. The agreement contains 20 articles and six accompanying photos.

Although negotiations were held with the British side, they were repeatedly postponed due to political changes. It is now scheduled to be returned before October 1st. Due to the relationship between body size, lighting, climate, time of day, indoor and outdoor, they have been able to create some different and novel dresses, no longer taking imitation as their ability.
